2018-01-13 09:07:54
Sharmita Bhattacharya
726062
5.0
India has become my most favorite place ever since I visited it on Thursday afternoon for a wholesome lunch with my friends. If Biriyani is the love of your life, and if you feel that you get the best of the lot in your Arsalans, it's time you give it a second thought. India's Dariabadi Biriyani which is one of their signature items is one of the best things I tasted this new year. Awadhi Biriyani on the other hand, isn't too rich, and is a perfect choice for those who want their Biriyani to be light. Talking about their Kebabs, the utterly delicious Galauti Kebab with Lucknowi Paratha is simply out of the world, making it the most desirable starter you could think of. Cheese Chicken Kebab is outstanding as well- big juicy pieces of chicken being wrapped in cheese this ensures that you are delighted and satisfied to the core. We also tried their Honey Fish, which was unexpectedly one of the best dishes I ever tried as a part of the Awadhi Menu. The use of honey and sesame seeds in an Indian kebab starter is quite unique and we all loved the way the whole dish tasted. Chicken Butter Masala and Chicken Masala were the unsung heroes, giving perfect company to our Dariabadi and Awadhi Biriyanis. Lastly, came in the desserts, Firni and Shahi Tukda- both were extremely well made and it was the perfect way to end such an elaborate and delicious spread. Next time I crave Biriyani or Kebabs, I am surely heading towards India, and you should too for all the right reasons. The ambience and service were really pleasant and we were served with a warm smile, which was the best part of our luncheon. Keep up the good work guys!!

##

2018-01-12 22:42:05
Somashri Ghosh
6541621
5.0
This place was in my wish list for long, fortunately I visited this place yesterday. Locating this was not difficult at all as it's just beside fancy market in khidirpore, the entrance is not that big but after you enter it's huge dining space will definitely amaze you. I just loved their theme, decor and the seating arrangement. The decor is aesthetic, with beautiful lights having mughal design, architecture is also reflecting the authenticity of the place.

The menu is pretty extensive it was difficult to choose from but I went with the suggestion, few trademark dishes of this place I chose to Hogg on. 

Galouti kebab- The kebab was so delicate that it was breaking while I took it to my plate, no doubt it had a melt in mouth consistency. Very rich with the umami and Mughal spices. It was served wIth Lucknowy parantha, again very soft and flaky.

Chicken cheese kebab- Chicken kebabs wrapped with layers of cheese served with pudina chutney and salad, the chicken pieces were moist and cheese was complimenting the chicken well.

Honey fish- Another delicacy, as I'm an ardent fan of seafood this dish was my most favorite one. The taste was very new for me, sweet and savory both and so delicious. 

Chicken Butter masala- Very rich consistency of gravy, soft and succulent pieces of chicken along with garlic naan was pretty good start to my main course. This is a must try for chicken lovers.

Chicken masala- This was fine tasted good enough, nothing special to mention about it, went well with the naan.

Mutton dariabadi biryani- This is a bit similar to hyderabadi style of biryani, very spicy and the quantity was huge, it suffices two person. 

Mutton awadhi Biryani- This dish is a signature of India restaurant, it comes in a sealed clay handi. When the lid opens the aroma of the spices makes your appetite rise to 100 then and there. I loved the rice texture and the fried onions were just adding a great flavor to the entire preparation. Mutton pieces were very soft and were intact with the juices, as it got the flavors from the Biryani. This should be enough to make me go visit this place again and again.

Firni- So balanced with the sweetness, taste was very good as it is made very traditionally, you can literally get the taste of kheer and rich milk cream. 

Shahi tukda- This was a great ending to my food hogging session and tasted just about right. 

The service was excellent and the staff were very courteous, they suggested quite well and I rejoiced my entire lunch scene at this restaurant. If you have time and think of having Indian food then India restaurant is a place you must not miss on.
Ps- Don't forget to order your glass of coke while ordering, it helps a lot.

2018-01-12 21:35:54
Dorothy Bhattacharjee
14346241
5.0
Just one word.. Perfect!
1) Starters - Honey fish (310 bucks) A bit to the sweeter side since it has honey..comes in 6 pieces with a few veggies and it's a dry preparation.

2) Main course - i) Awadhi Biriyani (350 bucks) Prepared in a clay pot and sealed with maida..when the lid is opened the aroma that comes out will fill the air..more than suffice for 2 persons..4 medium sized pieces o mutton lots of rice and a piece of aloo..a small bowl of raita is served with it.

ii) Mutton Rara Punjabi (270 bucks) Very delicious..it was recommended by the one who was serving us..and it completely complemented the Awadi Biriyani..4 medium sized pieces of mutton..and a baby potato..

3) Dessert - Shahi Tukda (80 bucks) Very yummy but till the dessert arrived we were so full to judge it's taste..

4) Drinks - One lime soda (60 bucks) and mohito slush (110 bucks)..the lime soda is just too common we always have..latter is strongly recommended..has a sweet sour taste..

Overall..India has crossed my level of expectations..each and every dish starting from the Chinese starter to the mughlai cuisine..everything was pitch perfect..
And they would add gst to the bill..that would be all..

2018-01-12 20:20:21
Archita Chakraborty
32290238
5.0
India Restaurant is indeed the legendary outlet of Kolkata which serves brilliant mughal delicacies. Their transformation is quite prominent with luxurious decor. The ambience is outstanding and it is a paradise for all biryani and kabab lovers! The restaurant is located just beside fancy market at Kidderpore. 
Coming to the food we had, 

üéÜ Honey Fish : Boneless fish pieces cooked with honey, onion, savoury sauces and chinese spices was the star of the evening. The fish was of best quality, soft , sweet as well as it had little heat in it. Honey fish was served with sated bell peppers and onion which gave the dish a different texture and taste.  

üéÜ Cheese Chicken Kabab : Chicken kabab coated with cheese and served hot. This dish should be eaten when hot. The cheesy affair with juicy chicken pieces is a big hit on their menu. The chicken pieces are sumptuous and worth every penny.

üéÜ Mutton Galawti Kabab : Minced mutton mixed with Mughal spices and fried to give a crisp exterior. The kabab was very delicious and rich in taste. The kabab was accompanied with hot Lucknowi parathas.

üéÜ Chicken Masala : Big chicken pieces with rich and creamy gravy and indian spices and garnished with coriander leaves gave it a hint of different favous. It was accompanied with Hot Garlic butter naan.

üéÜ Chicken Butter Masala : Boneless chicken made along with makhani gravy and lots of butter. This dish was served with garlic butter naan. The chicken was juicy and tender and the spices was right on point.

üéÜ Daryabadi biryani : Aromatic basmati rice cooked with two pieces of mutton, dry fruits, egg, and mixed with special spices. This biryani can only be found in this restaurant. This biryani us heavy, rich spices and dry fruits makes the luxury quotient higher. The mutton was very tender and tasty, melted in the mouth, the potato was soft and well spiced. 

üéÜ Mutton Awadhi Biryani : Aromatic basmati rice with four pieces of mutton, mixed with special spices and served in clay pot with raita. This biryani is light yet tastes like heaves. If you are a biryani lover then you will find this dish amazing and will want more.

üéÜ Shahi tukda : Soft bread soaked in kesar milk with perfect amount of sweetness. 

üéÜ Firni : My favourite kind of rice pudding. Great dish for all the sweet tooths of kolkata. 

I had a great experience with India Restaurant and will be going back these any time soon! ‚ù§

2018-01-04 14:44:32
Sourav Basak
2052714
4.0
Listend so much about this restaurant from zomato and friends. So decided to visit the place with friends when returning from holiday trip on 25th December, 2017. Let's jump to the review -
1. Order - Chicken biriyani, special chicken biriyani, Mutton biriyani, chicken reshmi kabab. There were so many quantities so skiped that part,just mentioned the dishes.
2. Location - This is the point where it lacks behind the other famous restaurants. Personally being a south kolkata resident khidderpore is pretty much far for dining to me.
3. Ambience - What an ambience. Just 2 stars for the interior itself. Just eye catching.
4. Staff courtesy - They were good to us. Even fulfilled our request to take a picture. Service was pretty fast. Just had a small rift regarding payments. We had told them to bill the delivery items separately, but we received the bill after paying the main bill so that lead to some confussion on both side.
5. Food - The kabab was lip smacking. I took the mutton biriyani and that was good but i had better biriyanis. The speciality of the biriyani is less oily and quantity. But what i liked most about the biriyani was the mutton piece. It was tender and well cooked, the best i have tested in recent years. The chicken biriyani was also very good as per my friends.
6. Pricing - This is not a place where you can expect damn cheap price but taking the ambience and food quality the pricing is value for money as per me.
Hope to visit again the place, there are so much left to try. Thank you for serving us.

2018-01-04 03:14:52
Tanusree Saha
38878424
4.0
AMBIENCE- 4.5/5
FOOD(Quality)- 3.5/5
FOOD(Quantity)- 3.5/5
SERVICE- 4/5
VALUE FOR MONEY- Yes.
RECOMMENDED- Yupp!!
This place was on my bucket list for a long time. So, went there on 20th December with two friends to celebrate the end of our exams. It was not at all difficult to find. From the moment we stepped inside, we had good vibes. The 1st and 2nd floor has an air conditioned set up and the ambience is mind blowing. We were seated at 1st floor but the 2nd floor is even better in terms of ambience I believe. So coming to the food:-
‚ö´Ô∏èChicken tandoori- This item failed to impress us. Being a tandoori lover I was expecting it to be better. The pieces of chicken were too small. And the taste was ordinary. The green mint chutney provided with it was sweet whereas I prefer it to be sour. So, it was a bit of a letdown.
‚ö´Ô∏èChicken biryani- Me and one of my friends took chicken biriyani. It was really delicious. The rice was well cooked and light with the perfect blend of spices. It was neither oily nor dry. The chicken too was very well cooked and juicy. Quantity of rice was more than enough. I could not finish it myself and my friend had to help me with it in the end.
‚ö´Ô∏èMutton biryani- According to my friend who had mutton biryani, it was awesome. She said that the piece of mutton was so well cooked that she did not have to struggle to cut the pieces with the spoon itself.
‚ö´Ô∏èFirni- We are not exactly fond of sweets after biriyani but I wanted to try the firni as I had seen people praise it in their reviews. So, though we were full, we ordered one firni and had a few spoonfuls. It was good but nothing extraordinary.
The service was prompt. The staff were cordial.
But, the tandoori chicken disappointed me. But I am willing to overlook it because the biriyani was superb. The prices are justified given the beautiful ambience. They charge 5% GST.
Overall, nice experience. Would love to visit again.
P.S.- They have a non-ac section on the ground floor for eating as well as takeaway. The menu is the same but the prices are about ‚Çπ20-30 less than in the AC section. Plus, there is no GST or any other tax whatsoever.

Mutton biriyani was perfect,not too much greasy not too much dry and with succulent mutton pieces.Mutton stew had succulent well seasoned meat chunks and the gravy tasted soo good. For biriyani lovers, it is highly recommended.

2017-12-28 00:02:03
Susmita Das
39671178
4.5
Located near Karl Marx Sarani, Kidderpore, this place serves truly legendary biriyani this town has to offer. The ambiance is undoubtedly wonderful, with a royal touch. It is grand and very spacious. Seating on the third floor is stunning. The feel of the place complements the food immensely well.  Service was prompt and very well-behaved. Extra points for such a courteous staff. Now comes the best part, FOOD. Dishes ordered -
1) Chicken tandoori - It was well marinated and just the right amount of char marks on it. The smokey flavor was not too strong. The meat was tender. (Rating - 4.5)
2) Chicken tikka butter masala (6 pcs) - The kebab pieces were tender and moist. Very well cooked and gravy was so so flavorful. The best chicken tikka I ever tried! Absolutely mouthwatering. Highly recommended! (Rating - 5.0)
3) Tandoori roti - It had a light sweet taste. Believe it or not, I could eat it as it is without a complementary gravy. Nonetheless, it went really well with the chicken dish mentioned above. It could be a bit more soft tho. (Rating - 4.0) 
4) Dariyabadi biriyani - THE biriyani is here. The taste was just spot on. Not too dry, not too moist. The flavors just explode in your mouth. It had some dry fruits which went really well, not like your regular biriyani. Indeed, one of the best biriyanis in town. Recommended! (Rating - 5.0)
5) Fresh lime soda - Very refreshing and sweet. This is the need of the hour after such a rich lunch! (Rating - 4.0)
       Going back for the Awadhi biriyani and firni and more, absolutely! If you're looking for ambiance and great food at a reasonable price, this is the place to go.

This place needs no introduction serving legendary biriyani since ages. You will get a royal feel as soon as you enter. Making us comfortable in the huge sofas we ordered

This instantly melts in your mouth and the taste is beyond amazing. The chutney served with it was a very different version of pudina chutney , slightly sweeter and amazingly complementing the dish. 

Mutton biriyani - The biriyani is not very rich in spices and the quantity is good enough for one person with good appetite. The mutton piece was well marinated and beautifully cooked. Though the 'aloo' in it seemed a bit bland. 

Tawa chicken - The gravy was too creamy and tasty with 6 big chunks of chicken. Though had to mention it was too oily and spicy but tasted heavenly. 

The best part was indeed the kabab. The service was pretty fast. The stuffs are well mannered. 
Definitely recommended.

2017-12-24 00:41:56
Supra Bhukta
276055
4.5
As a Big Time Food lover, I always wanted to visit this restaurant, though I had tasted their biriyani, but that time it was take away type order.

So finally I made my visit, to this awesome and new generation BIRIYANI joint in Kolkata.

Location : It is the heart of Kidderpore, Just beside the Fancy Market. So location wise people should not face any hard time to find it out.

Interior: Generally the difference what we are observing recent days, popular and generation old BIRIYANI joints are focusing on interior, so as INDIA. Well decorated stairs, spacious interior, vibrant color make the interior eye catching and smart.

Waiter:

All the waiters are well behaved, having decent knowledge about food.

Food:

We ordered below mentioned dishes

Peshwari Chicken Kebab:

Well cooked, soft, tendered, juicy and succulent six pieces of Boneless chicken with some Green Parsley Chatni and Salad.  Recommendable

Paneer Tikka :

Six pieces Paneer marinated with some grind spices, but this dish needs some improvement, I found the taste of Paneer a bit blunt. Something is missing, which i found. Not Recommendable

Mutton Galwati Kebab:

This is one of the dish which I was looking for, and I can say they did not disappoint me. 4 Medium sized Kebabs with Lucknow paratha is the perfect combination they had provided. The Kebabs are really soft, tendered and juicy with the feast of flavors. They are really melting in our mouth, so they did proper Justice to the Dish name as well. Highly Recommendable 

Mutton Awadhi Biriyani:

one of the signature dish of INDIA. This is a special order. People have to wait for 30 mins minimum. One Handi with 3-4 big pieces of Mutton, 3 Potatoes and Rice which is enough of Big Foodie like us. The Rice was well mixed with masala, not too spicy (Which way I Liked most), flavorful. 

Mutton pieces are well marinated and very very well cooked. Served with Raita (Which is refreshing)

So overall, Highly recommendable.

Price:

Overall price wise this is one the best cost effective BIRIYANI joint as well as perfect destination to taste some Afghan and Awadhian delicacy.

So Dear Kolkata and India Food Lovers, go and give a try in INDIA, (I Mean India Restaurant)

2017-12-17 10:13:24
Subhasish Bose
32070560
4.5
Me and my wife visited this restaurant yesterday with very high excitement as because we heard a lot about this place from our friends & colleagues. About there biryani, sahi tukra, kabab & firni. We ordered kaachi mutton biryani, awadhi mutton biryani, mutton pasinda kebab & sahi tukra. Unfortunately they informed us sahi tukra was finished and awadhi biryani would take extra 30mins. We was in bit of hurry so changed the order, an ordered mutton biryani, firni & gajar ka halwa. They served within 10-15mins. We was a bit of disappointed as didn't get the chance to taste the sahi tukra which is here's one of the speciality. Now come to the food part , both  biryanies was really good. Specially the kaachi biryani was awesome. Rice cooked perfectly, enough juicy and mutton was soft and well cooked. We taste most of famous biryanies in kolkata but this kaachi was the best we have so far.  Mutton pasinda kebab was moderate but the pudina chatni served with it was awesome. Combination of both was nice. Specially most of chatni serve with tandoori and kebab by other food chains in kolkata is very normal and monotonous. Firni was too good. Main good part with that firni was they didn't add any extra flavors or color. Taste was awesome too. Halwa was full of ghee and they served a bit of over heated but the taste was awesome. Ambiance was very impressive, stuff was polite and well behaved. Two things that disappointed us, that was the toilet that was very dirty. Second was the bike parking just in front of the restaurant is chargeable. That should be free. Except these overall was very good experience.

##

2017-12-16 21:50:54
Tathagata Biswas
440998
4.5
We drove 50km to try their food. I am pretty happy they didn't disappoint. The ambience is great. Perfectly lit, staffs are honest and courteous and food timings are appropriate. We ordered virgin mojito (green apple flavour), chicken cheese kebab(6), chicken chatpata kebab (10pcs), mutton boti kebab (6), daryabadi biryani (they said kachchi mutton biryani and daryabadi biryani is the same except the later has 2 mutton pieces instead of 1...umm okay!? ü§î Why change the name for an additional piece of boti?), Chicken chap, mutton kadhai, and to fill the dessert cravings we had shahi tukra and firni.

Review: Virgin mojito was impeccable and refreshing and delicious. The green apple and lime and mint packed a very refreshing punch! Do try it.
The cheese chicken kebabs were delicious, they do melt in your mouth. And the mint-coriander chutney provided was incredibly delicious. It's tart and sweet.
Chicken chatpata kebabs was just chicken wings in a partly spicy and tangy tandoori sauce. I wouldn't recommend this one. KFC is better if you want wings!
Mutton boti kebab was a bit tough and dry in itself but with the chutney, it went well.

Daryabadi (or kachchi biryani with an extra boti as they say,) was partly tangy and a little sweet to the palate. The acidity of the plums, the smokiness of the spices and sweetness of the cashews did overpower the meaty savoury flavour. If you like biryani just plain subtle and savoury, order the Awadhi one. And I must mention that the mutton was falling off the bone to the touch. Literally to the touch. That's how perfectly cooked it was!

Chicken chap and mutton boti (does have 5pcs in gravy) was nothing extraordinary. The gravy minus the thick oil/fat floating film was tasteful.

Shahi tukra did disappoint. It was just a boring piece of bread ( Heck! It lacked that aroma of ghee as a traditional shahi tukra should have!) Lying in a pool of mildly thickened milk with no garnish. This is the only disappointing item.
And finally firni soothed the disappointment. But I believe the quantity was less compared to others at same price. So -0.5 for the disappointing shahi tukra.
Overall, it does have the best brilliant biryanis and kebabs in town. Price is OK and is perfect for great group feasts. Do give this place a try!

Update on 9.12.2017:-
Received service at it's very best. This was pinnacle of customer service. I was called by the management of India restaurant. They apologized for the honest mistake. Sounded the same as well. Thumbs up for their responsible attitude towards customers.

2017-11-24 22:43:20
Sayan Majumder
43512827
4.5
Located at the most busiest place of kidderpore i.e fancy market, this restaurant will simply give you the feel of royalty and splendour with it's ambience...

The dining space covers a large area and is divided into an upper and a lower dining area...

Mughal cuisine being the speciality of this restaurant, we didn't hesitate to order most of their special Mughal delicacies...

The starter consisted of Indian special cheese kebab which was basically roasted chicken pieces covered with cheese slices and then fried as a whole... It was simply wow, being crispy outside and juicy inside along with the aroma of burnt coal...

For the main course, it was all about biriyani... Mutton biriyani , Kachhi biriyani and Awadhi biriyani...
The mutton biriyani was normal as in any other restaurant, with a large piece of mutton and potato which was sufficient for a person..

What was extraordinary about them was their Kachhi biriyani and Awadhi biriyani...
The Kachhi biriyani consisted of a large piece of mutton with potato and a boiled egg, made with perfect blend of aromatic spices and served with dry fruits...
The Awadhi biriyani was cooked and served in an earthen clay pot along with raeta... The ample amount of aromatic basmati rice with four pieces of mutton and potato will easily suffice 2 people...

For the side dish, the waiter suggested us Chicken tikka butter masala which consisted of 6 pieces of chicken tikka cooked with rich mix of spices and butter(you will have forget your dieting for a day)... The creamy texture of the dish along with the aroma of earthen oven made it perfect for accompaniment...

The dessert included Shahi tukra(which was also one of their special items) and Firni...

The service was pretty good, with a quick refill time... The waiters were very friendly and explained us each and every dish...
Pocket pinch is moderate..

Must try dishes are the Kachhi biriyani, Awadhi biriyani and Shahi tukra...

If you are in kidderpore, don't forget to drop by this restaurant... You won't be let down for sure...

2017-11-11 20:42:54
Shayenki Kanjilal

5.0
This was my second visit to this heavenly place. This time we were there in a group of 7. 

This place has a majestic ambience with a beautiful interior, specially the staircase! There are many mirrors on the walls which give it a very nice and attractive look.

The staffs are always humble. As we enter, the guard welcomes us with his smile and also greets goodbye as we leave the place.

We had some noteworthy dishes... and here they are..
üëå Flavoured Mojito
üëå Chicken cheese kabab
üëå Mutton barra kabab
üëå Daryabadi biryani
üëå Lucknowi laccha paratha 
üëå Tawa chicken
üëå Fish tikka butter masala
üëå Firni

Mojito ~~ this is a refreshing drink of many flavours with mint leaves and ice, sliced lemon and cherry on it which gives a catchy look when served.

Chicken cheese kabab ~~ this is a speciality of this restaurant. The kababs are rolled in cheese layers and they taste just yummy. Tha kababs are also soft. they serve this with a green chutney and salad. 

Mutton barra kabab ~~ i have not tried mutton starters before. But this changed my taste. It tasted much like tandoori with mutton. Pieces are medium size and are with bone. This platter also comes with a green chutney and some salad.

Daryabadi biryani ~~ i love biryani and this is a special biryani with a unique taste. Unlike normal biryani this dish have some hidden secrets in it. The biryani had 2 mutton pieces, 1 egg and a potato. Also it is a bit spicy but well garnished.

Lucknowi laccha paratha ~~ it was soft and big size paratha. Tasted nice on served hot.

Tawa chicken ~~ very yummy, mouth watering dish. Pieces were medium size and the gravy is spicy with an authentic taste. It goes best with lucknowi laccha paratha.

Fish tikka butter masala ~~ tried fish item after a very long time. This Indian item of fish is a wow wow for me. Fish pieces are very soft and tasty. The gravy tasted awesome. Its a must try for everyone.

Firni ~~ aww... i am a desert lover and firni is my love. But i have tasted the best firni here. It tasted like kheer and seems like it almost melts in our tongue. Heavenly feeling. Happy ending with sweet tongues..

I am overwhelmed by the services as well as the food. We all enjoyed the grand lunch. It was an honour for me to be a part of this gathering. Will surely visit this place again...

üò∫Fish tikka butter masala-I am not a fan of fish dishes when it comes to north indian but you could just give this one a try for that distinct flavour of the fish coming through.Garnished with cream and coriander leaves on top this was a surprise entry to my list of favourites
üò∫Lucknowi paratha-Crispy and paper thin layers comprised of this one.Pair it with any creamy non veg item and you are good to go
üò∫Firni--A perfect finish to an awsome meal ,yummy smooth as silk bowl of goodness.

Thanks team India Restaurant for the warm hospitality and for a tout into the world of lip-smacking delicacies.

2017-11-10 11:34:53
Ishita Chatterjee
34859262
5.0
An Amazing place with some amazing dishes. 

Yesterday, I with few of my friends visited this place, and we ate to our heart's content. We had a number of dishes and each one of them pleased us.

Here is a glimpse of what all we had.

Flavoured Mojito Slush - 3 different flavors were served, each one was super refreshing. 

Chicken Cheese Kebab - This was my very first time tasting cheese kebab, and it was cheesy enough to make me say cheesy things like, "This is the most delicious chicken kebab I have ever tasted." 

Mutton Barrar Kebab - Though it says mutton, it is basically 4 medium sized lamb pieces with some tandoori spices roasted in an oven. It has that typical tandoori taste to it, which makes your taste buds go gaga over it.

Daryabadi Biriyani - To be honest, I am not a biriyani fan, but this made me re-think my choices. Never have I ever tasted a biriyani as great as this. This is a must try one. The sweet aftertaste that it leaves on your tongue, is something that you are surely going to remember for a very long time. It is one of their special biriyanis and is available only on Thursdays. So, if you are visiting on a Thursday, do not forget to order this.

Lucknowi Lachcha Paratha - It is usually served with Galawati Kebab, and is not mentioned on the menu, but you can always ask them separately for it. This particular paratha, is a lot like the base roti of rolls( egg roll, chicken roll), but is a lot less oily and a lot tasty. Tasty to such extent that I kept eating it without any side dish. 

Tawa Chicken - It is a lovely dish for all those who don't like too spicy food. Yes, it does looks spicy, but when you taste it, you can actually feel the cashew gravy, which subdues the hotness of the dish.

Fish Tikka Butter Masala - Another amazing side dish. The Tikka smell prolongs and makes you eat it more and more. It was spicy and tasty. Also, the fish was cooked perfectly. 

Firni - Ending such a sumptuous lunch without a bowl of Firni sounds like a sin. So he had our share of Firni, and well, India Restuarant made me fall in love with Firni once again. The thick-set firni, wasn't too sweet and was the perfect ending to that amazing lunch that I had.

To sum it all, this is a worth visit and worth recommending place. The interior is beautiful, and the staff is courteous making you want to re-visit.

##

2017-10-28 11:40:13
Oishik Sarkar
3119605
5.0
India Restaurant is one of the most highly rated Awadi restaurant in Kolkata. Mainly famous for their Biryani, this one is very easy to locate at Khidirpur near to fancy market.

Decorations :
==============
The ambience over here is none less than than a 5 star luxury hotel. The restaurant is very large divided their dines into 2 separated floors. Each of the dining is also very large & can handle a lot of people at once. Everything from lights to decorations, from cushions to tables all are premium. Their beautifully designed ceiling is eye catcher. Warm white lit ambience & their luxury cushions are very comfortable.

Staffs and Management :
=======================
India Restaurant has taken care of all the aspects to become a good restaurant. All their staffs are well known of this & maintain the professionalism. Their service was fast & great. We had the following in the foods...

Tandoori & Kebabs :
=================

Chicken Malai Kebab (4/5) :
-----------------------------------
Chicken Malai Kebab was garnished as beautifully as their ambience. In a plate only 6 pieces of chicken was present but that of big size. Unlike other places their Malai Kebab was not creamy rather it was dried. Kebab was grilled very well with the perfection in it. Kebab tasted very good that gave us the true awadi feelings. Green chutney served with it was lite & tasted more like curd.

Mutton Seekh Kebab (4/5) :
-----------------------------------
Visiting North Indian Restaurant and not having Mutton Kebabs isn't what foodies like to do. So, we didn't missed this dish. This dish looked delicious in a shape of sausage. Also it tasted kind of different than expected. This kebab was made by minced mutton in a shape of sausage and then grilling it. It was red, hot and spicy to taste with very lite smoky flavour.

Fish Tikka Kebab (4/5) :
-----------------------------------
6 pieces of Fish Tikka Kebab, red, spicy and juicy inside. Fish was extremely soft and well cooked and the mix spices made this kebabs so rich that fish didn‚Äôt smelt like it. Take it hot without any sauce and mind is blown with its flavour.

Mains :
========

Butter Naan :
-----------------------------------
It was traditional Butter Naan as per their standard, soft, well baked and tasty. Naan was also big in size and matched well with their side dishes.

Chicken Afghani (4/5) :
------------------------------
Julienne cut chicken with afghani rich hot red spices, Chicken Afghani is a great dish to have with Naan or rumali roti. Unlike other places their chicken afghani isn‚Äôt much hot, its flavour was little bit different and really enjoyable.

India Restaurant's Speciality :
======================

Murg Mussallam (5/5) :
-----------------------------------
Now comes the star dish of India Restaurant. Actually each and every dish over here is star but this one is beyond that and Murg Mussallam is nothing less than heaven for a foodie like me. Yes a whole big sized chicken is cooked in this dish and it needs to be ordered at least 2 hours before. In this 2 hours they made an incredible dish that also tasted incredible, looked incredible. When it was served, It was huge for a single person to finish. It was targeted for the mad foodies like us. A full chicken, full of spices inside it floating in ghee and colourful salad around it was just attracting us to come and eat it. Wow! It tasted incredible, it tasted awesome, it tasted great. Hands down no comparison, its the best ever Murg Mussallam I‚Äôve ever tried. Gravy was made of keema and its brilliant spices with their butter naan, no words can explain this experience.

King of Mughal Dishes The Biryani :
=========================

Mutton Biryani (4.5/5) :
-----------------------------------
Its their regular Biryani & it was made the best way possible. It also tastes one of the best among all the famous Biryani restaurants in Kolkata. 1 big Mutton piece and one potato nothing to expect more in this package. But this mutton piece and potato was perfectly cooked as expected. With its authentic flavour and smell, their is basically no comparison of it. Personally I like this biryani much more than their Awadi and Kacchi Biryani but one thing that dissatisfy me about this is its quantity. The quantity served in regular Mutton Biryani is excessive less, just a flat layer of rice on plate. Forgot about dividing it to 2 rather one needs at least 2 plate of it for feeding hunger. Whats this India Restaurant, you surely need to focus on it.

Mutton Awadhi Biryani (4.5/5) :
---------------------------------------
Served in a true Awadhi style, Aromic long grain basmati rice with four pieces of mutton in a clay pot it is for spice lovers. The special spices used in this made it really rich in taste. Same quality of mutton, soft and juicy but with added spices and its richness. The yellow and white mixed colour texture of this biryani inside of the clay handi looks beautiful and one of its kind. It is the true Royal biryani someone can wish over here. This biryani doesn't need any side dish, just the Raita they serve with it is enough.

Mutton Kacchi Biryani (4.5/5) :
---------------------------------------
Kacchi Biryani is one of their most famous dish & here is why. It was mixed with some rich dry fruits with some brilliant rich spices mixed in appropriate order. Not only that It tasted totally different than the regular Biryani, little on the tangier side I would say. The portion was average, the Mutton piece was big & very deeply cooked. It was soft just like it should be, potato was also well cooked. The balance of oil was also noticeable. I had coke in soft drink menu with it, that also was served very well making this combo perfect.

Sweet Tooth Desserts :
====================

Firni (4/5) :
----------------
Firni is what people love here after their wonderful Biryani and its their most famous and most selling according to Zomato. Undoubtedly I loved it too, and as its home made by them only, so its hard to find the same density elsewhere. Also its sweetness is remarkable, an absolute recommended.

Shahi Tukra (3/5) :
------------------------
Its one of their special and most selling dessert too. But personally I didn't liked this dish much. Well balanced Kesaria flavour and sweetness was nice but the bread in the middle wasn't matching the whole dish. Well that was my personal preference, you may try it.

Pricing :
========
Their pricing becomes bit expensive after added taxes for the quantity they serve. Where overall experience over here is worth every penny you spent.

Conclusion :
============
The best thing over here is their newly made beautiful decorations. The ambience is perfect for family dinner as well as a special date. Not just that their Biryani is also remarkable. I recommend this place to every Biryani lover out there.

On this auspicious festival of lights and colors, we visited to Indian Restaurant, Khiderpore to celebrate the festive of sparkling lights Diwali with a Mesmerizing course of Menu !!

Indian cuisine is about as easy to explain as thermodynamics. India has welcomed a multitude of settlers with a variety of belief systems. In order to understand the evolution of the indigenous cuisine of India, one must realize this country is anything but homogeneous. Regions and religions make up a large portion of the cultural fabric of the food. ‚ÄúIndian food‚Äù has been coined a phrase by the diversity of it‚Äôs food is as diverse as it‚Äôs people.
It's ambiance perfectly denotes the Indian and Mughal style way. So, the staffs are courteous and impeccable to serve there customers.

We had,

‚Ä¢Fish Tikka Kabab - Tandoori fish tikka is a famous non-vegetarian snack and made in Indian style on BBQ or grill. The fish doesn't lose the tender taste from inside yet tastes crispy on the outside. The key is to marinate the fish well. 

‚Ä¢Mutton Seekh Kebab - Mutton seekh kebab is a delighting non-vegetarian starter popularly relished as side dish in India. You can find it across street stalls or dhabas but this place serves the best Kabab in all. Being a mutton delicacy, it is cooked slowly on a BBQ or grill so that the kebabs come out soft and perfect. The mutton is ground with spices mix and made into balls that go into the oven or on tandoor via skewers.¬†

‚Ä¢Chicken Afghani - Afghani Chicken Curry is a delicious chicken recipe from Afghanistan. Rich in spices, this recipe tastes best when served with rice or roti or Naan.

‚Ä¢Butter Naan - Butter Naan, a butter flavored flat bread is one of the most extremely delicious dish of Indian breads. This is usually made in¬†¬†tandoor,¬† can also be made on¬† stove¬† top¬† and¬† oven. ¬†
Mostly, we get the chance to relish them in restaurants or in parties. It came out absolutely YUMMYY¬† with that melt in the mouth flavor..:)

‚Ä¢Murg Masallam - Murgh Musallam¬†literally means whole chicken. The dish was popular among the royal Mughal families of Awadh, now the state of India.
And the India restaurant serves the best murg mhsallam, and make you feel the flavor of Awad.

‚Ä¢Mutton Awadhi Biryani - Biryani¬†‚Äì¬†even the word sounds so delicious and exotic, smells aromatic and promises a royal treat of highly fragrant¬†basmati¬†rice and richly spiced succulent meat, dish that is fit for kings and nobles. Though the word ‚Äúbiryani‚Äù which is derived from the word ‚Äúbiryan‚Äù has its root in Persia, the dish is known to origin in India during Mughal dyansty rules. As the saying goes that ‚Äúnecessity is the mother of all inventions‚Äù so does the biryani which is invented to feed the huge Mughal armies during the war times. And as the Emperors and their Kingsmen shifted, conquering regions as they go, the flavour of Biryani began to transform, incorporating the local flavours and and now we are blessed with so many regional versions of biryanis in India, each one with different taste profile. No matter from where or how it has originated, Biryani is one such dish that has able to unified our country in some sense and with its brimming aromatic flavours has touched the soul of every Indian.
Mughal biryani in Awadhi or Lucknowi style - a rice and meat dish that is known for its head aroma and fragnant of spices.

‚Ä¢Firni - It¬†is a¬†rice pudding¬†from the cuisine of the¬†Indian subcontinent, made by boiling rice, broken wheat,¬†tapioca, or¬†vermicelli¬†with milk and sugar; it is flavoured with¬†cardamon,¬†raisins,¬†saffron,¬†cashews,¬†pistachios¬†or¬†almonds. It is typically served during a meal or as a dessert. It is also known in some regions as¬†payesh,¬†payasam,¬†payasa,¬†phirni,¬†gil-e-firdaus¬†and¬†kheer.

The diversity of it's food is as diverse as it's people. We left very full! I‚Äôll definitely be back.

Phirni:-(5/5) one of the best phirnis in town. The taste of sweet didn't overpower the dish and was well balanced.
I would definitely recommend this place. Will visit the place again for sure.

Rudradeep Biswas (RDB)
2910482
5.0
Among the top biriyani makers of Kolkata, India Restaurant at Kidderpore needs a special mention. In spite of located at a quite odd place, India Restaurant draws biriyani lovers from all over the city and beyond.¬†

They have three floors - ground floor is like a dhaba, eat and out. While upper two floors are lavishly decorated interiorly and have AC. However I don't mind whether they have AC floor or not, until they continue to make excellent Indian cuisines.¬†

What do they offer: Kachhi Biriyani is their top seller. Come after 3:30 pm and you will miss it. But they have some hidden gems which often people miss it like - Awadhi Biriyani, Daryabadi Biriyani. And I am telling you that both are awesome. Daryabadi is bit more spicy than Awadhi, but both come with tender mutton botis.¬†

They make excellent Murg Massallam, Fish tikka kebabs and Mutton Seekh kebabs. Murg Massallam, as the name says, is a entire chicken stuffed with masala, is baked and served as a royal dish. It takes around 4 hours to make and serve. Totally yummy!!! Kebabs are superb, tender and would make the perfect starter of your dine out.¬†

As I had Chicken Afgani and Naan too, I would mention that they are equally good, but being a biriyani lover, I can't put these rooti and side dishes at par with India's biriyani offerings.¬†

India has been offering several deserts - Firni, Sahi Tukra and Gajar Halua. But Firni is best, almost zero dalda/moida and super smooth texture.¬†

In case you missed India Restaurant, visit ASAP!

5.0
This is the apt place for all the people who call themselves food lovers.And even if you are not a food lover ,this place will make you one.It is one of the legendary outlets in kolkata that serve the best dishes you will ever have.It's actually a paradise for food enthusiast.Located very conveniently in khidderpore,this is a gem of a place and you will regret missing it.

The place is very thoughtfully created with a royal touch to the interiors and will make you feel like you are in a palace surrounded with soulful and lip smackingly delicious food.The ambiance and decor is the best in every sense.The creative 3D art work was mind blowing.Spread over ground + 2 floor, this place is spacious enough,the ground floor being their takeaway counter .The staff was extremely helpful and courteous.

Moving on to the¬† main aspect -FOOD

We started with,

1.Mutton seekh kebab-The kebab was extremely delicious and flavourful. Perfectly cooked with a balance of spices is my description for this delectable dish.Pudina dip and salad is also served with this starter.

2.Fish tikka-It was succulent ,juicy and totally melt in mouth.This one is made with delicate basa fish marinated with spices and cooked with love.Indeed the best fish tikka i have ever had.Highly recommended.

For the MAIN COURSE,

1.Mutton awadhi biryani-Served in clay pots and sealed with wheat flour dough,this is gonna be the best biryani you will ever have.The biryani had 4 juicy and tender mutton pieces and was a bit on the spicier side.The long rice grains had the perfect aroma of spices and each bite of it will¬† make you long for more.

2.Murgh Musollam-This one is a very special dish and requires to be cooked for 2 hrs on dum.The whole chicken is stuffed with egg and is cooked with lots of aromatic spices and that makes this dish amazing.The gravy is made with chicken keema and lots of cashews.

3.Chicken afghani-It had chicken juliennes cooked till perfection.The taste was simply amazing with balanced flavours .This gravy dish is the perfect side dish with the right consistency for any type of naan or roti.

4.Butter naan-Naan was very soft and not all chewy.The¬† naan was brushed with generous amount of butter to retain its softness.We enjoyed every bite of the naan with the delicious side dishes.

5.Phirni-Any meal is incomplete without desert.So for desert we opted for their popular phirni. Served in a petite clay dish,the phirni was totally different from the other places as it was more creamier and the texture was awesome.This one is totally recommended.Caution-Miss it at your own risk.

The pocket pinch was also reasonable for the delicious food they serve.If you haven't visited this place yet you are seriously missing out something big.So visit ASAP.

A big thanks to the whole team of India restaurant for their outstanding service.I would love to visit this place again and again and i am sure each time i will be back with another bunch of memorable experience.

##

2017-10-08 11:47:31
P.R.CHOUDHURY
2570124
3.5
Went to India restaurant yesterday, after ages.Today it is a 300 seater restaurant (possibly one of the biggest in capacity in Kolkata) with "semi fine dining" (if one can say that) ambience. The central A/C works very efficiently indeed. It has become multi-cuisine, with Chinese being a part of the menu.

It was pre-decided that we shall have the Indian cuisine & ordered a reasonably large menu.

Started off with Galawati Kabab (4 kababs of very decent size/plate) served with a complimentary "Lucknowi paratha" (thin paratha fried with very little oil). The kabab & paratha were absolutely divine. Almost took me to "Tundey" Lucknow. Almost, because the flavour quotient was lacking a wee bit. The portion served is good for 2 persons.

Followed it up by Chicken Afghani kabab & was floored. Soft, succelent, medium sized, 5 pieces of pure bliss. The flavour was subtle & tasted sublime with that signature smoky aroma.

Wanted a Shammi kabab (I am not aware if any outlet makes it any more) which was not listed in the menu. Was recommended Kakori instead. This was a let down, since it was the same "galawati mix" done up on a sheek. The taste of "grounded bengal grams" was completely missing.

Followed this up with Chicken Tangri kabab, which was a let down again. Too spiced up & cooked in very high heat. Thus the surface was burnt, crusted & bitter.

This was followed by Mutton burrra kabab. Yet again too spiced up, cooked in high heat, crusted & burnt exterior.

All the portions were large & good for 2 persons. An added advantage was the option of "half plate" for some kababs.

Then came the two biriyanis, we had ordered. The "Mutton Biriyani special", which is the regular biriyani, with two pieces of mutton. This is a lovely work of art, with a very fine balance between the aroma & spices.

The piece-de-resistance was the "mutton awadhi biriyani". It is only prepared upon order & has a half hour lead time. Served in a earthen sealed pot ...... ohhh!! the aroma when the seal was broken. Trust me, even the guests on the next table turned around. Light, fluffy basmati, cooked in dum with whole spices defines culinary bliss. The 4 pieces of mutton was soft, succelent & boneless. Also has an Alu.

The dessert was firni of course & without any doubt & hesistation, I would rate it the best firni I have had in Kolkata so far. So much so that we packed four firnis back home.

Overall, it is an outlet today, which is basically designed to serve a large number of guests at one time & hence some dishes maybe lacking in the taste quotient to the discerning tongue.

Ideally, one must instruct the steward to slow cook the kababs (especially mutton varieties) & I am sure the best can be obtained. I for sure would visit this outlet once again, to get the best results.

In the end, let me remember Chef Avatar Gill, of Astor Hotel ((Kabab-e-que), whom old timers like me may recall (alas he is not there any more). I am yet to taste a mutton burra kabab, like the way he made.

MUTTON KAKURI KEBAB: Holy cow! KACHHI BIRIYANI: Well after hearing a lot about it and following the waiter's recommendation we ordered this item accordingly.This Biriyani is same as the DARYABADI BIRIYANI except the fact that the later comes with 2 pieces of mutton.This Biriyani had cashew nuts and raisins with the plum(aloobokhra) which gives it a very unique flavour.My expectation was a bit more about this Biriyani because it was highly recommend by the waiters and other people in the F and P department, however I did not like the sweetish and sour taste of rasins and nuts with Biriyani.Anyway it was a little okayish.I would have rated this place 5 but the Biriyani disappointed me.
GAJAR KA HALWA: Again this was really well cooked. The aroma of ghee with every spoon of the halwa was really mouth watering.
SHAHI TUKRA: This dessert was also very delicious.Again another peice of perfection.Highly recommended.

2017-10-05 23:38:09
Petuk Baba
790102
5.0
In the hustle bustle of Khidirpur, India Restaurant stands tall like a renowned culinary wonder of kolkata. India restaurant needs no special introduction to the foodies of kolkata specially those who are fond of north indian cuisine. The location of this place is fairly easy since its just a 2 minutes walk from fancy market and also on the main road which makes it fairly simple to locate this place.

The outlet has 2 floors of AC sitting. We were seated in the first floor which has a huge sitting capacity and can easily pack loads of customers. But the what attracted me was the decor and ambience. Shiny furnishing along with usage of right kind of lights surely would make your dining experience a very royal one. The place has separate wash basins & toilets which makes this a very customer friendly place since many places lack these basic amenities.

Anyways cutting back to chase, I shall mention about the culinary treat we were experienced with:-

1. Virgin Mojito - A very refreshing basic virgin mojito served with with mint leaves & a dash of lime with a cherry to top it off. The dilution of the mojito was spot on since it had the perfect zing to go with our lunch. Loved every bit of it.

2. Macchi Sarsowali - 1 plate of this kebab comes in 4pcs. This was certainly the star of the kebab section. Made with delicate basa fish with absolutely gob smacking marination made us crave for more of this dish. Pudina chutney & chopped salad as accompaniments were given with the kebabs. Highly Recommended dish which one must not miss!!

3. Chicken chatpata kebab - 10 pcs of chicken wings marinated in spicy tikka masala were given 1 plate along with pudina chutney & chopped salad. Foodies having love for spicy tikka kebabs must try this dish. The taste was simply outstanding in terms of balance of flavours & the cooking of the kebab was absolute perfection. Another recommended dish!!

4. Chicken malai kebab - 6 pcs of kebab comes in 1 plate along with pudina chutney & chopped salad. This version of kebab was rather light & amicable in taste compared to the previous 2 kebabs but still won our hearts with its taste & delicateness. The taste of malai was felt in each biteful.

5. Paneer Tikka kebabs - This was consumed by our vegetarian group member. According to him he had one of the best paneer tikka kebabs ever in kolkata due to its sheer softness & marination of the masala.

6. Butter Naan - Our main course started off with naans along with non veg side dishes. The naans were fluffy with generous amount of butter being brushed over the naans to maintain the moisture. The naans were were too good to eat due to the soft nature of it which indicated the quality of its preparation. One fact which caught my attraction was that the naans remained soft even after some moment of time(like about 10-15mins) due us being taking snaps of it.

7. Garlic Naan - Same texture as the butter naan with only difference being the presence of garlic chops & herbs instead of butter. The garlics were in generous portions & certainly was enjoyable with our side dishes.

8. Chicken achari - The chicken side dish of our main course. The lovely smell of achar(pickle) tickled our nose buds before we dug into the dish. The dish had 4 pieces of medium sized chunks of chicken with a nice non spicy gravy. The gravy was absolutely delectable with right amount of consistency needed to compliment our naans. We were absolutely thrilled with the dish. Definitely recommended.

9. Mutton dakbanglow - A bengali's meal is just incomplete without the presence of a rich mutton dish. So mutton dakbanglow was there just to savour the whole moment of our lunch. Again 4 pcs of soft juicy chunky muttons were given in the dish along with a boiled egg. The rich gravy surely was contrasting to the chicken one. We kept on licking our fingers after having this dish. Surely a crowd pleaser this dish.

10. Mixed Vegetables - A traditional mixed veg which is an absolute favourite for any foodie.

11. Special mutton biryani - A north indian outlet's main challenge is always to pass the biryani test amongst its customers. A good/bad biryani can really make/break a place specially in kolkata where customers just swear by their love for biryani. The quantity of the biryani was certainly on the higher side which had 2 pcs of large mutton pieces,1 egg & 1 potato. The biryani was spicy and the rice had a beautiful aroma to it but the mutton deserves a special mention due to its sheer tenderness & taste. Although i felt the biryani was a tad too overly spiced.

12. Veg biryani - The presentation certainly caught our eyes & the quantity was also very generous. A bowl of raita was also provided along with it.

13. Firni - Now coming to the desserts we started off with the classical firni. The firni was certainly different as compared to other places since it was a bit dense but packed with lots of flavours as a firni should be. Loved every spoonful of it.

14. Shahi tukda - This dish was the only flaw i felt in whole of our meal. The texture of the dish was certainly too light which i think was due to the addition of rosewater. But no hard feelings.

After our hefty lunch we certainly left with a happy potbelly and a smile on our faces. Also a big thank you to Vicky Chen and the whole team of India restaurant for the warm hospitality & the service. A special mention to Tanmoy Basak for all the arrangement. So head down to india restaurant asap to enjoy some magnificent north indian cuisine.

5.0
When it comes to Biryani & Mughlai food India Restaurant is one of the best places , if not the best , in Kolkata . In all my earlier visits I opted for the takeaway option &  today is my first visit to their dine in facility . Located just beside the Fancy Market in Khidderpore area the restaurant can be identified from a distance .Today being a Monday we did not face any problem with  parking as the area was less congested than other days . The ground floor has seen some facelift but the huge surprise was waiting for us upstairs . The beautifully decorated interiors , adequate lighting , comfortable seating caught our eyes . Whoever has designed the place deserves great accolades for keeping in mind even the minute details like having a separate entry for staffs . The staffs attending to us greeted us with warm smile & were attentive to our demands throughout . Having had  such a warm welcome we were eagerly waiting for our foods with high expectations & ordered the following taking advise from the ever smiling captain .
Gallowti Kabab : My all time favourite dish when it comes to Kababs. Here it is actually a combo of 4 pieces of Kabab with salad & Lucknowi Paratha . I had heard from a renowned Chef that it takes a combination of 32 spices to prepare Gallowti . I do not know how many spices they use but whatever they use the resultant product is simply mouthwatering . My eyes got closed as I enjoyed the beautiful smell & taste of Gallowti . The Paratha itself is very tasty & the synergy with Kabab is spellbinding . 
Mutton Awadhi Biryani : Having tasted their normal Biryani on a number of occasions ( they are equally good too ) this time opted for this variant . The captain politely informed us that it would take about 20 minutes to prepare & serve the dish . The Biryani came in a earthen pot & contained 4 pieces of mutton , 2 pieces of potato , Raita & beautifully aromated basmati rice . This is totally different from our very own Kolkata Biryani . The rice was nicely cooked , the mutton pieces were soft & our senses were filled with beautiful smell of spices - really an amazing experience . The quantity is sufficient for two persons .
Dum Chicken : The captain suggested this to us & we were glad that he did as this was the best of the lot . The dish contained 4 big pieces of chicken in a red gravy . The chicken had become tender & almost melted in our mouth . The spicy gravy was brilliant . My own feeling is that this dish will be stunning with Nun & I will surely come back to try it out again .
Firni : Good quality of Firni - a must for me after having a Mughlai meal .
Shahi Tukra : The Malai associated with  right dose of saffron was mouthwatering . A great dessert . 
Overall a greatly satisfying experience with definite pledge to come back & try their other delicacies . Highly recommended .

Located just few step ahead of Fancy Market which is the tech & fashion hub of khidderpore this mighty place will welcome you with all its glory. Hugely structured & charmingly decorated this place gets a thumbs up for ambience and space. Now, the reason for which we went there,
‚Ä¢Chicken Tandoori Kebab: very juicy very tender in one word lip-smacking, got our tastebuds running.
‚Ä¢Chicken Biriyani: comes first in zomato for 'brilliant biriyanis', I must say it was quite a hype. Tasted better biriyani elsewhere too. No such surprises.
‚Ä¢Chicken Tikka Butter Masala: cubes of chicken tikka cooked in thick red gravy went well with both biriyani & roti.
‚Ä¢Rumali Roti: its out of the menu order, yeah they serves bread. I must say haven't seen such big roti anywhere else. One was enough for me.
‚Ä¢Firni: mughlai cuisine can't get over without this. One of the best firni in town, even portion was good. Highly Recommended.
Had a cold drinks too which i think is not worth mentioning.
They don't serve you in a fancy or innovative way like other places but they will please you with the taste they offer, no doubt in that. Very reasonably priced for such a location. Points cut for limited chicken options in biriyani & courteousness in service which was highly disappointing. Still worthy a place to come & have typical mughlai cuisine to crackle the tastebuds.
P.S.: they serve breads like nun, roti etc which is not present in the menu, & chinese options are also available.

Overall the ambience was good, the waiters were less attentive and the food was decent.

##

2017-08-05 12:06:03
Arnab Mitra
1939476
4.5
India Restaurant, as "larger than life" the name suggests, has a "large than life" substance in it too, and we got to feel that when we decided to drop by for a sumptuous lunch on the last Thursday(27th July) afternoon. This is one such place which literally poked me from my wishlist for long. And that's the precise reason for which I was primarily up for it even when we had to change our route only for a lunch at this place.

LOCATION :
Located at the Khidderpore junction (Watgunj More) and beside the Fancy Market, India Restaurant is a landmark by itself in that area. It's a 2-storey building with the ground floor having a Non AC accommodation and shabbier like other normal biriyani joints. However, the game changes altogether when you climb up to the 2nd storey. Its as plush as you can get in a Mughlai and Awadhi restaurant and that too in Khidderpore area, is a never-seen-before phenomenon. They have a separate sophisticated lounge area to wait for your turn, as they are primarily filled up during pick hours.

FOOD :
Coming to the food, I always had benchmarks to beat in every cuisine and the one who surpasses the benchmark becomes a benchmark itself. Such a phenomenon happened that day. Below are the item-wise details along with the feedback :
1. Mugh Chatpata Kebab - One of the most simple yet brilliant kebabs I have ever had. Served with green mint and yoghurt chutney, this is a chicken wings' kebab with tandoori spices, which leaves a tangy aftertaste. Highly recommended.
2. Galawati Kebab - The legendary Galawati is served here with Lucknowi paratha on the house which make things even sinful. The Galawati reminded me of Aminabad (Lucknow) and its texture distinctly proclaims that it's creator is a pro in this genre. One of the most authentic version of the dish is found in this place in Kolkata and one is ought to try this to feel the real flavours of Lucknow. Highly recommended.
3. Mutton Awadhi Biriyani - The staff taking orders recommended us to have Kachchi Biriyani, but don't know what happened to my sixth sense that I went for this. Served in clay "handi", this may disappoint you if you are seeking a legendary Lucknowi version of biriyani. The mutton and potato is as soft as ever. However, I personally didn't like the taste and texture of the rice.
4. Fresh Lime Soda - Brilliant ! Had two glasses of it ! :)
5. Shahi Tukda - One of the best I ever had, and there is no second thought to it. The bread is the softest it can possibly be, and the sweet is not overpowering. It had generous amounts of almonds too.
The bill was about eleven hundred and something which was very justified compared to the quantity of food we had.

SERVICE :
Without a tinge of exaggeration, I would say that I have never seen such a cordial service in a restaurant serving Mughlai and Awadhi cuisine. There were 3 staffs attending us in tandem and all of them made us feel like home with their heart-warming smile. For an instance, we were keen on sitting at the window side table while we could see that the window side of the restaurant had stopped operation by that time of late afternoon. But on our request, we were instantly escorted to one of the tables of the window side and a staff had been appointed to that area. That's a big big learning for all other restaurants and these small things make your customers loyal.¬†

In all, there are still some uncharted corners left in the vast sea of offerings that India Restaurant has in its kitty, but the experience I had here is one worthing remembering and something which had already made me loyal to this place. To all Mughlai lovers of this city, try out this place at least once as this place is all set to make milestones in the Kolkata food scene.

P.S. Try out the Mutton Kachchi Biriyani and do let me know how it tastes, so that I can try out in my next visit ! :)

Have heard so much about this place that I had all decided in my mind to definitely visit this place before leaving Kolkata. Located at the heart of Khidderpore, this place is famous for its biryani. My sister had brought me for a treat over here. Earlier this place was a shabby one and how they have revamped this place! A royal classy decor extending over two floors with a huge waiting area, India Restaurant is surely going to catch your eyes. 
Service was very warm by all the staffs and it was quite efficient and prompt. 
For food, we had ordered - 
Mutton Galawati Kebabs - A Lucknow classic. This  was really good when being served with parathas. I loved it! 
Prawn Malai Kebabs - Very tender prawns marinated in a yogurt served with a mint chutney was extremely good. Recommended to try. 
Kachchi Biryani - Every single person I met who suggested me to try this restaurant also suggested me to try this out. I heard that this dish gets over by 7pm. But really? Is this biryani worth so much hype? It was so oily, so spicy, came with too many dry fruits (who uses that in an Indian Biryani?) and none of us in my family or me liked it. Disgusted with this, we had taken a normal plate of Mutton Biryani and it was amazing! I would suggest to try this plain Biryani at India Restaurant and not the Kachchi one. Oh please, not at all worth it. 
Firni - At the end of a huge disappointment, came little platters of happiness. Made out of jaggery and retaining the perfect grainy texture, it's truly one of the best I have had in a while. 
My overall experience at India Restaurant was good. I would like to come back here again for the firni and definitely not the overhyped Kachchi Biryani. That's it! Happy Dining! :)

2017-07-24 19:17:39
Anindita Ghosh
1025083
4.5
Visiting India Restaurant was another step closer to ticking off some of the best restaurants in town, from my bucket list.
Situated right next to Fancy Market (Kidderpore), the area is congested enough to drive you crazy when it comes to park your car.üòè
The place remains full even on weekdays! We went on a Thursday night and the two floors were already jam packed with people still waiting for their turn. Since we had already booked a table earlier, it wasn't much of a deal to grab a table for 9.
The ambience is really good with well lit lights and white and golden glossy decor.

Coming to what we ordered and how we felt about the food:

1) Mutton Kakori Kebab @Rs.270.00 (4.5/5) :
We couldn't just dine-in in India Restaurant and miss the famous 'Kakuri Kebab' here. A plate consisted of 4 cylindrical long, soft, melt-in-the-mouth portions of well made kakori kebabs. The meat was so damn delicate with brilliant depth of flavours which would keep you thinking about what spices have been used to actually make it that delicious. Each bite was a stupendous journey of aromatic spices and distinct flavours in the mouth. Definitely recommended. üòç

2) India Restaurant Special Chicken cheese kebab @Rs.320.00 (3.9/5) :
Again a very well made portion of chicken reshmi kebabs topped and baked with generous amount of gooey cheese.üòã
The kebabs were well charred and the cheesy layer was baked to perfection.
It was fantastic but I prefer the cheese kebabs at Arsalan, a tad bit more. üòÑ

3) Chicken Chaap @Rs.180.00 (3.25/5) :
The chicken chaap failed to impress us..üòè Everything about the chaap was good but it lacked the tang or pungency that is required to illuminate a well made Chaap. The meat was very soft and well cooked, though.

4) Laccha Paratha @Rs.35.00 (4/5) :
To be very honest, no matter how unhealthy it sounds but I prefer the deep fried old-school Laccha paratha over the modern layered tawa grilled laccha paratha üòè and, the paratha here was exactly the deep fried version that I love.üòÑüòÉ
Thoroughly took pleasure in the process of wrapping the thick fried doughy goodness around kebabs and dunking them in green chutney before eating it.üòã

5) Chelo Kebab @Rs.370.00 (3.5/5) :
Chelo kebab happens to be an Iranian dish which has been indianised and served here. 3 delicate pieces of chicken tikka kebab, 2 pieces of chicken kakori kebabs, stuffed tomato, grilled onion and a fried egg served with buttered rice. üòç
While the chicken tikka kebabs were too good, the chicken seekh kebabs were a let down because they were more or less pretty tough to be called a proper seekh kebab.

6) Mutton Awadhi Biryani @Rs.350.00 (4.95/5):
The briyani came in a traditional earthenware sealed with dough. On opening the seal and top of the pot, the ghee laden aromatic smell made us sniff till the spoonfuls of biryani were in our mouth. Oh! What an amazing biryani it was! Words cannot describe how beautiful it was in terms of flavour. Eat it, to believe and experience what it like to taste heaven.

7) Special Mutton Biryani @Rs.310.00 (4/5):
We did not want to restrict ourselves only to Awadhi Biryani, hence we ordered two more varieties - one being a normal biryani to just know the difference between their version and the other big biryani making houses of Kolkata. The biryani here was pretty darn good with soft beautifully cooked mutton, an egg and obviously the delicate potato.üòç
The rice grains were independent and the biryani wasn't very oily as well. Super liked it.üòö

8) Daryabadi Biryani @Rs.330.00 (4.25/5) :
Daryabadi biryani was mentioned as a must-try on Zomato so we just ordered a plate of this, to be on the safe side and not get gifted with curses from around because this biryani was supposed to have a sweetish masaledar tinge to it with cashews, nuts and raisins. We were a bit apprehensive when we received a plateful of Daryabadi Biryani garnished with tomatoes (üò´üòíüò≤) but soon after our tastebuds started dancing to the harmony of different flavours! I would ask Kolkata Biryani loyalists to stay away from Daryabadi Biryani because this was so much different than what a biryani usually is like but nonetheless, my father and I totally relished it till the last morsel of rice.üòç

9)Firni @Rs.60.00 (3.85/5):
We wanted Shahi Tukda but ofcourse, given to my sad luck, it wasn't available. With a heavy heart we ordered Firnis. The firnis were great, with a strong taste of rabdi but the firni which my aunt received tasted pretty different from the ones we had. The one my aunt had, tasted more like the ones from Lazeez, Arsalan, Shiraz. Otherwise, the firni was pretty good.

10) Fresh Lime Soda @Rs.60.00 (3.5/5) :
Tasted normal.üòÑ

The total bill was Rs.4310.00 for 9 people which is around 478.00INR/person which is quite reasonable given to the amazing food taste and quality.

Final Conclusions:-
‚óèFood Taste Rate = 4.25/5.
‚óèAmbience = 4/5
‚óèStaff Behaviour = 4.5/5
‚óèValue for money = 4.5/5

Definitely recommended!üòÑü§ó
Happy eating.
Stay beautiful. ‚ù§
Eat.Salivate.Repeat

4.5
It's located just beside the fancy market in khiderpore on the road moving towards the dock. Previously it was a bit shabby but after it was remodeled, the interior design and the ambience of the place is one of the best in the city. The ambience of the place is truly Mughal and it complements the dishes that are served in the restaurant. The staff behavioral is very polite and good. They help you to order and will never mislead you. Coming to food, in starters I tasted chicken malai kabab and mutton Boti kabab. The malai kabab was very well cooked and drained was awesome. The Boti kabab was also well prepared but I felt a bit over cooked and was a bit stiff. On the main course, the place is known for the iconic biriyani they serve. I have  tasted chicken biriyani, mutton biriyani, mutton kacchi biriyani and daryabadi biriyani. Chicken and the mutton biriyani does not contain egg where the other two variant contains one each. The meat is very well cooked. The kacchi biriyani and the daryabadi biriyani contains dried fruits. I felt the daryabadi to be the spicy counterpart of the kacchi biriyani. As a side dish, the kadai chicken was also well cooked and a bit spicy, perfect to be had with nun and not biriyani. Whereas the tawa chicken was perfect for biriyani. As a desert, the firni was also good. The quantity of all the dishes are good for an adult with moderate appetit. Definitely visiting the place again.

2017-07-06 08:23:22

4.5
Went to India Restaurant for the first time for my mother's birthday‚Äã on the 5th of July. Our order was:
Chicken Malai kebab, Mutton Seekh kebab, Galawti kebab, Mutton kadhai with tandoori rotis, Mutton Biryani and Shahi Tukda.
The kebabs were awesome and getting to taste them straight out of the Tandoor just elevated the flavours. Galawti and Seekh kebabs just melted in the mouth. The Galawti kebab comes with a complimentary paratha which was soft and light. Then came the Mutton kadhai which was a bit spicy along with hot tandoori rotis. The biryani was spicy but nice and if you want the mutton piece to be changed, they will do that without any hesitation. In our case the waiter sir changed the piece on his own while serving. Then came the Shahi Tukda which everyone recommends is a must have. The bread was soft and juicy after sucking on the milky broth and the plate was greased with the reduced broth. I know many would love to hang me for this......but the Shahi Tukda which my mother makes tastes much better.
All in all, the food was top class, the waiters were well behaved and the interiors are royally done ( great place to click photos). We enjoyed the evening laced with beautiful memories......and we look forward to be back there soon.

4.5
After a lot of planning and debate, two of my best foodie friends and I made our way to this joint after walking all the way from Rabindra Sadan. We took our seat in the first floor and the first thing that strikes is the ambience. Feels like you're in a different world altogether. The order was simple: Mutton Boti Kebab, Mutton Kakori Kebab, Mutton Awadhi Biryani (they had run out of the Kachchhi Biryani which was our target) and Shahi Tukda.

The Kakori Kebab was something like I've never had. It just melted in my mouth. It was just too good to be true. Oh! What a beauty!
The steaming hot biryani in the handi was just a festival of flavours and it was so rich. It literally felt like what the Nawabs would've had. The added fried onions was the bonus.
Now, I had never had Shahi Tukda before so it was a new experience for me. I dug in and what I was greeted with was probably one if the best tates that exists in the world. The texture of the tukda with the flvour of ghee and the gravy packed with milk, condensed milk, kheer and saffron was something beyond extraordinary. Sheer brilliance! I licked my plate absolutely clean so that they need not wash it again.
And one of the best and weirdest things was that they didn't charge any tax but we didn't mind leaving behind a tip as a token of appreciation. Thank you India Restaurant. Please open more branches everywhere!

All over its a nice place if you visit the upper floors but the ground floor lacks discipline from both staff and management because even the guy on the cash counter was busy all the time with his ph talking to someone and noticing nothing on the ongoing services over the tables. 

Will visit again for a better experience to the newly built upper tiers.

2017-05-19 12:20:57
Swagat Mohapatra/Local.food.ideas
29257246
4.5
Follow me on instagram @local.food.ideas for more food updates üòçüòã

Visited kolkata for a short food trip, After reading so many positive response and blogger's recommendation decided to give it a try and trust me it is worth it. Easily one of the BEST restaurant in Kolkata. Coming to food we ordered, :-

1- Kachi biryani - It was different from other regular biryani. Mutton pieces were properly cooked and dry fruits like cashews you can find in the rice, overall you can't afford to miss this biryani preparation. (5*/5)

2- Dum chicken - 4 Big leg pieces of chicken, you'll have hard time to finish it if you are alone . Bit spicy and semi gravy. Best to have it with naan or Lucknowi Paratha. ( 4.5*/5)

3- Mutton kadai - Bit on oily side but thick flavourful spicy gravy with boneless mutton pieces makes it worth it. ( 4/5)

4- Mutton biryani - Regular mutton biryani With one big mutton piece. Quantity was more than enough for 1 person and taste was awesome. ( 4*/5)

5- Chicken bharta -  Shreaded pieces of chicken with white gravy made up of cashews n other dry fruits and boiled egg mixed together . Definitely must try. ( 4*/5)

6- Mutton Galawati Kebab - The most famous dish of this resraurant, 4 pieces of minced mutton kebab served with Parathas is a must try. You can't afford to miss this dish if you are visiting this restaurant. ( 5*/5)

7- Phirni - Desert dish , It is available in most of the resraurants in Kolkata but India restaurant makes it the best ( 5*/5)

8- Shahi ka tukra - Desert dish, A must try . Make sure you arrive early to have this. (5*/5)

Negative remarks -
-.5* Mutton kadai was bit on oily side , can be improved.
Overall verdict - ( 4.5*/5)

2017-05-02 10:48:16
Dipannita Mallick
27871309
5.0
Visited this place fot the second time yesterday on a special invitation from team India Restaurant and I just fell in love with the place. The restaurant looks beautiful and it is very spacious as well.
Coming to the food, I had ordered for Chicken Cheese Kebab, Awadhi Biryani and Shahi Tukda all of which I wanted to eat from this place for a really long time. And also had a tall glass of Fresh lime soda which was very refreshing.
The Chicken Cheese kebab had chicken along with the goodness of cheese. It had 6 large pieces. The kebab tasted amazing. The chicken was cooked to perfection and the cheese added amazing flavours to the entire dish. The kebabs were served with salad and the mint dip. The mint dip was really good. It was not too tangy neither too bland. It had a perfect balance of everything and went really well with the kebabs. The kebabs had the perfect taste and I would recommend everyone visiting there to try this one out. I am sure this wouldn't disappoint any foodie who loves to eat kebabs.
Then came the Awadhi Biryani in a handi along with raita. The awadhi biryani has 4 pieces of mutton and 2 pieces of potatoes though I am not sure about the number of potatoes, it may be more in number. Anyway, the biryani is well enough to serve 3 people it is that great in quantity. The biryani was made with finest quality of rice and it was lip-smacking. I had tasted awadhi biryani previously in another popular place in kolkata but after yesterday I can tell undoubtedly that the awadhi biryani of India was way better. It had perfect royal taste. Perfect blend of spices and the ghee added to the flavour of the biryani. The mutton in the biryani was tender and cooked to perfection. I didn't have to struggle to tear the meat off the bones, it was that well cooked.
Coming to the dessert I chose Shahi tukda because I am not much into firni. And boy I made the correct choice. The shahi tukda came with a large piece of bread and amazing malai. It was just perfect. It wasn't overly sweet or had too much essence. It was an amazing ending to the meal.
Now talking about hospitality, I think it has one of the most courteous team I have ever come across. After I reached I was greeted so warmly by their floor manager Waseem. He made sure I was comfortable and was very attentive. Other service persons were also very well trained.
I would like to mention here that there are very few restaurants who actually care about the kind of experience their customers had. I had a rough experience on my previous visit and their management is so effective that they took note of the experience and did not hesitate to apologies and show how much they care for their customer's culinary experience. They made up with the food and service this time and I had an amazing experience.
And a big thank you to Joydeep Sen (of marketing department) for being present there and making my experience in India Restaurant more amazing.
I would recommend everyone to visit this restaurant and go through an amazing culinary and hospitality experience. üòä

The bread was soft and the chicken pieces were quite tender but the gravy disappointed me a lot. I had better in my previous encounters. ¬†

All in all, this place is hugely recommended for the biriyani lovers. Surprisingly the VAT and service tax is included in the menu which is great. I would definitely visit this place for their Awadhi biriyani. ¬†
