##

2017-03-11 18:50:52
Debashish Dey - Petukbangali.com
424506
4.0
To those mughlai food lovers to whom Arsalan and Aminia are benchmark of good biryani destinations , you need to magnify your search and come here and get bowled over by the awesome quality and ambience of a "Good Mughlai Restaurant " . India restaurant has really come a long way their basic outlet to a luxury fine dining one just on their top floor . It's not my first time here but I could not open down my last awesome experience here so finally came here and doing it . 

¬∞ Location :-  Located exactly on the heart of kidderpore . Beside fancy market . If you are coming from ola/Uber then the destination won't be an issue . But if you are not then look for fancy market in kidderpore .

¬∞ Ambience & Service ( 4 / 5 ) :- A fine looking interior for a classic fine dining mughlai restaurant . The ambience is top notch and something you will immediately notice on entering .The staff is well-dressed, polite and very helpful . The serving time for the kabaabs was around 7 minutes , the biryani came after 10 minutes and the desert took another 7 minutes .

------------------------------------------
¬∞ Food :- No mughlai restaurant is complete without it's splendid array of kabaabs and although we were spoilt for choice we still managed to select 2 mind blowing kabaab starters .

1. Chicken cheese kabaab. ( 5 / 5 ) :- Simply mind blowing . One of their specialties and a must ordered item . Generous portions of  boneless chicken covered with tandoori spices and grilled after topped in a cheesy coating . This is as good as it gets . If you someone who really loves a spoonfull of cheese with your chicken then you must have this please . 
6 cheesy chicken kabaab pieces for 320 rupees is a steal deal .

2. Mutton galawti kabaab ( 5 / 5 ) :-  Just stunning . Minced mutton lovers or more specifically galawti kabaab lovers this is the real thing for you . For once move over oudh and have a bite from here . 4 generous pieces of minced mutton delight served with 4 crispy and light paratha . A statutory advise is to taste it with you eyes closed because you will be simply blown away . A must must order .

After getting blown over by the kabaabs , we were really hungry for some biryani . And here we made a mistake . We were 3 guys and all of us ordered the same dish instead of going for variations . We went for the much celebrated kacchi Biryani as neither of us were ready to miss out on the much famed dish from this place . And here is my take on it .

3. Kacchi Biryani ( 3 / 5 ) :- Okay so a low rating . Let's just start the discussion on what kind of biryani I like . I am a big fan of Kolkata biryani or those who are very much close to it . I am not saying that the other biryani should try to replicate that but I am.also saying that the whole appearance of biryani in my head is fixed on the Kolkata biryani so anything close to it will be appreciated by me but anything deviating far from it is a tough thing for my appetite . And the most important turning off for me was the over indulgence of ALU bokhra in the kacchi Biryani which made it tangy . It may be welcome for other biryani lovers but for me it is not really welcome . The potato , rice and mutton everything was tangy and I could not continue with the dish and gave up half way.  I know this dish is carrying a lot of sentiments and good regards from a whole lot of lovers of this dish but frankly this biryani is not for me and those who are an avid lover of the Kolkata version and have a hard time experimenting, please don't go for it . I would not stress much in the quantity much , the rice was of good quality and quantity and the meat was succulent but everything was tangy . Go for kacchi and dariyabadi biryani only if you fond of tangy spices in your biryani .

4. Firni ( 4 / 5 ) :- A perfect firni to end a mixed mughlai food experience . The texture was fine and the taste spot on .

5. Gajar ka halwa ( 3 / 5 ) :- Not the best halwa I have had . Poor in quantity and the taste was okayish .

----------------------------------------------

¬∞ Verdict :-. A must must visit for the mughlai lovers . A word of advice for the Kolkata biryani lovers that they should only go for the normal special mutton biryani and not experiment much . Other than that the kabaabs are simply out of the world and the place is suited for a fine dining mughlai experience .

Its located on a very busy street of Khidderpore. Inside decoration is without a doubt top class. And one of the mocktail ordered was horrible (though cheap). Service was again normal given the heavy rush at the restaurant.The menu price include the VAT and service tax amount. So you pay only what is mentioned on the menu.¬† May be I would like to visit this place again on a quite weekday evening but definitely not on a sunday eve.¬† So in short India Restaurant is a place with Decor of a Hotel The Park but with food, service, etc of Arsalan/Aminia Restaurant.

2017-02-09 20:03:46
Bitan Banerjee
291684
5.0
I went there for an office lunch with my team. Located very near to Fancy Market in Kidderpore, India Restaurant is definitely the crowning jewel among all the Mughlai restaurants in Kolkata. The interior will give you a very royal feeling. The place is almost crowded due to its immense popularity most of the time. We were a large group, so it took some time to get the seats. The food ordered by us was eclectic: chicken biriyani, mutton biriyani, galoti kebabs, chicken reshmi kebabs, chicken malai kebabs, tandoori roti, parantha, rumali roti and mutton. The biriyani was like ambrosia, amazingly fragrant with no trace of excess oil and greatly cooked meat. The kebabs were succulent and brilliant. The tandoori roti was soft and hot. The mutton gravy was spicy and perfectly cooked. The rumali rotis were excellent. For desserts we had firni: just amazing!! This place is highly recommended for all the epicures!!!

2017-01-30 13:35:17
Samarpita Banerjee
30173944
4.0
We went to India Restaurant hoping that we would be able to have their famous Kacchi Biryani. Little did we know that we were headed for big disappointment. As luck would have it, they had run out of the biryani. Anyhow, we refused to get disheartened and do all in our might to make it worth the visit. We were successful. We were a group of eight and we ordered a lot of food ranging from chicken Malai tikka to galauti kebabs to Awadhi biryani to rezala and Julian chicken. Would like to write on each item individually. The malai tikka, while not having a lot of malai proved to be a hit. It was soft and succulent and the right amount of spicy. They served the galauti kebab next with which they also gave us a few parathas. Now we being stupid, we thought they were supposed to be a part of the main course. After having the galauti kebab one of us picked up a little piece of the paratha to taste it, only to realise it was an accompaniment. And the paratha was one of the best things about the restaurant. It was crispy and soft at the same time and the taste was amazing. Our only regret was we didn't have it with the kebab as we were supposed to. While I have had better galauti kebabs in the past, the ones at India Restaurant came pretty close too. They had that melt-in-the-mouth texture as all such kebabs are supposed to have. Next came our main course, we loved even the naans and butter naans that were served. Very soft. We ordered both chicken and mutton rezala and it was very light and cooked the perfect amount. The only catch was it only had one piece. I wish they would have more pieces. We also ordered Julian chicken which tasted more like Kadhai chicken. This was the only dish, other than the Awadhi biryani that I found a little underwhelming. The biryani according to me was a bit too wet and I didn't much like the spices. We ended the feast with firnis. I wish they had the shahi Tukda. The firnis were quite good too. I would recommend IR and please do eat the galautis with those magical parathas.

I think that India restaurant serves one of the best Biriyani in town

I went there on behalf of PanchPhoron team on the occasion of Iftar special Food Festival @ ¬†The India Restaurant .

We were served the following -

Mocktails ‚Äì¬†

1)Deep Blue Sea

2)Pineapple Blossom

3)Strawberry Blossom

4)Mango Blossom

5)Choco Cocoa-

6) Virgin Mojito¬†

My picks -
All mocktails looked presentable and were well made & refreshing. But I found Strawberry Blossom the best. Highly recommended......!!

Foods ‚Äì

1. Paneer kurkure

2. Beguni

3. Peyaji

4. Galaouti kebabs with lucknawi Paratha

5. Special mutton haleem

6. Chicken reshmi kebab

7. Fresh fruit platter included watermelon, banana, pineapple , papaya & mango.

8. Egg chilli tossed with peppers

My picks - Though all the items were well cooked and yummy but I preferred the following the most -

1) Egg Chilli tossed with peppers- It was lipsmacking, flavourful . A perfect high protein juicy snack.

2)Paneer Kurkure - It looked like spring rolls, it was crispy outside & soft inside and was palatable. I couldn't resist myself from having more of it.

3) Chicken Reshmi kebab - It was succulent, flavourful and very tempting.

4) Special Mutton Haleem- A very important dish made of meat, lentils, spices etc cooked for a long time and is a protein packed food. It was well cooked and yummy.

5) Peyaji- A popular telebhaja, it was less oily and crispy .

Enjoy the pious Iftaar with your friends and family here or come here on any other day and relish. It would be definately worth it.

Thanks to the management for hosting us and their hospitality.

3.5
On last Saturday evening, we decided to visit this place. The zomato score of 4.4/5 was inviting us for quite some time !¬†I had called to book table and I was¬†politely told that booking¬†is not needed and¬†we will get a seat even without booking.¬†We found paid¬†parking¬†space close by.The air conditioned dining place is in second floor but for aged people there is a lift. Interior is beautifully done. We started with gilawati Kabab which was served with a complementary parantha. Good, very close to the north indian standards but taste is bit hot and spicy. So those who donot like spicy and hot stuff should avoid this.¬†Next we¬†ordered a plate of chicken malai kabab for the child in the group and a kabab platter for rest of us. The kakab platter had 5/6 variety of kababs , two pieces of each item. It included prawn tandoori and mutton tikka as well. Once done we reordered the platter. At around 9.15 pm we wanted to order another plate of malai tikka but it was over. Being Saturday evening, which I felt is too soon a time for items getting exhausted. We settled down for Reshmi Kabab. But any day the malai tikka is juicier and softer than its counter part. Kababs were good, rather I must say very good. Now you may be wondering why 3.5 then ? Well we were disappointed with the main course. We ordered Awadhi Biriyani which was served in a earthen pot, having 4 medium sized mutton pieces and two medium sized potatoes. The mutton was uncooked. It was pretty hard. We reported the manager and he took back the 4th piece and replaced it . But the replacement was equally hard. Given the score of 4.4 I am not sure if it is always the same or the day we visited it happened. We had also ordered afgani chicken and laccha parantha. Parantha was layered and crisp but afgani chicken was disappointing, The¬†chicken was hard and fibrous, nowhere near the mouth melting experience of kababs. The salt in the dish was also high. Therefore I would advise to concentrate on kababs when you visit this place. By the time we reached desserts Sahi Tukra was¬†not available. We settled for Gajar Ka Halwa, which was average.¬†They serve mocktails¬†but ice-cream is not available now. ¬†For five adults and one kid the pocket pinch was around Rs.2,700.

##

2016-11-04 20:08:32
Souvik Ghosh
6791311
5.0
India Restaurant, Kidderpore

If you really want to know the meaning of transformation, you need to have visited India Restaurant in its early years and at the current time. What started out as a small outlet serving biryani and kababs has now turned into a plush, two storied fine dine restaurant. They have done up the place beautifully, and thankfully, the quality of the food has not dipped, in fact it felt that it had improved quite a bit from what my memories of childhood brought back. Maybe it was just the ambiance, cannot be completely sure!

Well, cutting back to the story, or rather the food, we started with the Mutton Gilawati Kabab and Chicken Peshawari Kabab. It must be mentioned that I consider Gilawati to be the best kabab in the country, and I am very apprehensive to have it outside Lucknow, lest it destroys my untarnished love for it. My experiences in Kolkata i.e. Oudh 1590 and Naushijaan had been average, but having read so much about the version at India Restaurant, I did go for it. We paired the kababs with a couple of Lucknowi Parathas. The Peshawari Kababs were the first to arrive ‚Äì chicken lollypops done in the tandoor with a white marinade, with malai and a hint of garlic. They were quite good, and helped fill up waiting space for the Gilawati. The parathas were very well-done, and were appropriately saved for their soulmate, which arrived in due time. The Gilawatis looked quite bigger than their Lucknowi counterparts, and my first bite was tentative and expectant. As it turned out, India Restaurant does know how to make these! The outer layer was crisp and caramelized, while the inside was a mash of mutton and lentils and papaya juice that just melts in your palette and creates magic. The taste was superb and it actually came very close to what I am used to having in/from Lucknow, even if the outer texture is a little different.

Recovering from the bliss, we ordered a Mutton Dariyabadi Biryani and Chicken Rezala for the mains. The Dariyabadi Biryani is nothing but Kachhi Biryani ‚Äì a version of the rice preparation made with raw mutton from the start. The biryani was excellent ‚Äì a little different from the usual Kolkata biryani, a little richer and the spice blend was not the usual one ‚Äì nonetheless it tasted superb. The mutton was the best part of it ‚Äì tender and falling from the bones on a little probe. The Rezala was awesome as well ‚Äì the gravy was rich and slightly sweet ‚Äì just the way I like it, and I drank some of the gravy like a soup, meting out the treatment a great Rezala gravy deserves. Of course, it was a little too rich to finish, and about half a bowl of gravy was whisked away on request before I could sip it all, and I daresay that meant a little less stress for my arteries. Anyways, it was a great great meal and I insist all folks in Kolkata travel to the port side of the city to give these guys a visit. Highly recommended.

##

2016-08-27 19:46:03
Debajyoti (www.foodiedada.com)
1855976
4.5
If you are a Bengali, you must have heard the term ‚Äògobor-e padmaful‚Äô, I won‚Äôt take the pain to elaborate the meaning which is pretty clear to every Bengali, but if you are not a Bengali then let‚Äôs put it pretty bluntly for you ‚Äì this place called ‚ÄòIndia Restaurant‚Äô somewhat stands in debris, in a pretty unruly environment filled in with chaos and in a not-so-clean locality of Fancy Market, Khidirpore. In the last few months it has undergone some civil ‚Äòplastic surgery‚Äô work which has made it look like the ‚ÄòShilpa Shetty‚Äô of Biriyani Houses in the town :) So, you can‚Äôt really ignore her!

Jokes apart, the interiors of India Restaurant are now simply stunning. It feels as if you are at some mansion in Dubai and you are at some party or dawat maybe, hosted by some super wealthy Sheikh! From the moment you enter this place you notice super clean marble flooring with embedded motifs and walls with lining of glowing signature tiles. The strategically lighted circular false ceiling designs have become quite a trademark of this place by now. If you climb up the stairs and reach second floor, you get to see more of the building and you‚Äôll discover it being immensely well-maintained, clean, brightly lit with an ultimate glittery finish that leaves you overwhelmed. From Interior decoration point of view, the place gets full marks for all that royal finish, no doubt about that. Seating arrangements are well spaced out and the chairs and couches are very comfortable as well.

But this multi-storied glittery pot of gastronomical gems is quite hard to commute, and it is really tricky to find a proper place to park your car at this place. So the only saving grace is the abundant availability of Uber or Ola, but then I am not sure if I will take that pain to take a cab and come down all the way, traveling the entire breadth of the city just to have a plate of biriyani! Well, I used to think like this unless I learnt about the range of biriyanis they serve and their characteristic flavors. And after I saw some latest pics of this place, I decided to pay them a visit sometime very soon. But still it got delayed, due to the odd location of this place and the poor parking facility. Finally, the day came when I had to make it to India Restaurant since some of the food bloggers from Panchphoron (including me) were invited to this place by their management. So as pre-decided, I took a cab and reached the place on a super-gloomy day for lunch. I was quite astonished to discover the volume of crowd dining at this place on that weekday late-afternoon in such an unpleasant weather outside. The footfall surely indicates the quality of food being served at this place, so I became more hopeful about the food and expectations kept on building!

Now without wasting any further precious words of mine, let‚Äôs delve deep into the food talk where the crux of the matter lies! So, here are the items which I had tried at this place -

MOCKTAIL

a) Virgin Mojito ‚Äì I had heard the mocktails served at this place are amazing, but sadly most of the mocktails were not available that day. Apart from the North Indian or Mughlai fare they also put equal amount of importance on mocktails and infact on every dish which they serve. In fact the simple Virgin Mojito was too refreshing to be true! The sweet balance was perfect, just a bit lemony with a dash of mint, packed with crushed ice and heavily refreshing! And yes, the presentation was simple yet appetizing with slices of lemon and cherry on top. Surely you can try this out here.

STARTERS

a) Chicken Cheese Kababs ‚Äì These are deep brown colored kebabs with a smooth outer texture and were quite fragrant to elevate your appetite. The chicken pieces in there were very soft and it clearly shows how well they were marinated. As the name goes, it was quite cheesy and had a mild spiciness to it; also it was cooked in tandoor to perfection thus locking all the juices inside.

b) Mutton Galawati kababs ‚Äì Well, if you have already tasted Oudh‚Äôs Galawati kebabs then you might be tad disappointed here, but still I must say these are close competitors to Oudh‚Äôs Galawati. Here at India, the texture of the meat paste (which is really creamy and having a dash of zafran in it) was perfect. It looked nice with those flattened meat ball structures. It tasted nice with those thin layered paranthas which were served along with it. But the stuff was tad overdone with the outer skin showing evidences of it, having few hardened or rather burnt spots.

c) Pineapple Tandoori ‚Äì The stuff tasted awesome, to start with. The large slices of pineapple were very well cooked in tandoor after it was marinated with lemon juice and spices for hours. The final product had all the juices of the pineapple locked inside it, that was fresh and succulent as it should be and tasted awesome with that sweetness of pineapple, tanginess of the spices and that smokiness coming after it got tandoor-ed. Awesomeness redefined!

MAINS¬†

a) Daryabaadi Biriyani ‚Äì The main course had five variants of biriyani, and Daryabaadi Biriyani was the one we tasted first. This Daryabaadi biriyani has a very typical taste which you can‚Äôt judge or comment without tasting it, it is unlike all other variants. The aroma was so unique and pleasant. Daryabadi Biriyani is surely the signature dish of India Restaurant and it has got fragrant mildly spicy flaky rice, sweet potato and super soft juicy piece of meat! Together they taste awesome! Must try!

b) Kachhi Biriyani ‚Äì Again a gem of a dish served with all its honesty and subtle flavors in one amazing plate. Here they put layer of raw marinated meat on a layer of raw basmati rice before they are cooked together. The also have the spices and the a yogurt based marinade layer at the bottom, here they also add the sweet potatoes, these layered structure is now left to cook in slow pace in its own steam. The kachhi biriyani overall has a yellowish color and a very subtle flavor, nothing too aromatic or flavorful, the subtle aroma which it has got is beautiful and majestic. The mutton pieces are extremely well cooked and literally melt in your mouth!

c) Awadhi Biriyani ‚Äì The Awadhi biriyani was served in the earthen handi in which it was cooked. It tasted just amazing to be honest. We were almost lost in that strong aroma of ghee and zafran. This method of slow cooking in the dum pukht style where you seal the handi with wheat dough always locks the awesome flavors and drives the biriyani enthusiasts and foodies crazy when the dough is removed and the lid is opened, the same thing happened with us as well! And somehow we ended overeating this gem of a dish for its rich yet subtle flavors and insanely good aroma! Must try!

d) Chicken and Mutton Biriyani ‚Äì There were separate plates of Chicken Biriyani and Mutton biriyani which were so called cooked in ‚Äònormal‚Äô style and these are the ones that we have most of the times from all the biriyani shops or houses. These were nice as well, nice aroma, not too oily and the meat pieces were well cooked.

Overall, I will rate India Restaurant close to 8.5 out of 10 for its authentic, amazing flavorful biriyanis and the variants which are available under one roof; not to forget the awesome ambiance and friendly service. Only the location and the communication is bit of a headache which I guess can‚Äôt be cured so easily. So, to sum it up if you haven‚Äôt yet tried India and you are a Biriyani lover then you are surely doing something wrong, this is a place you should never ever miss if you are in Kolkata. If possible try their Daryabaadi, Awadhi and Kachhi Biriyanis which you won‚Äôt get at every Biriyani shop, they are really well prepared and are amazing. Hopefully you will enjoy your meal here, it has got loads of potential to satiate your taste buds, so make sure you reach the place before the wheat dough is removed and the lid gets opened :)

Cheers!

2016-08-09 13:10:13
Ankur Banik
737186
5.0
For quite a long time now, I was itching to try out the new renovated India restaurant, having heard rave reviews from fellow foodies and friends alike. After a few failed attempts, I finally managed to visit this place a couple of days back and had a gastronomic experience to savor.¬†

Located right beside the kidderpore fancy market this place has been serving up decent Biryani and North Inidan food for a long long time. This was my first visit to this place after it has undergone what seemed like a major makeover. The place has a non ac section downstairs and an ac one in the first floor. The moment you enter the stairs it seemed like a world far far away from the busy,crowded and not-so-sophisticated locality. The majestic interiors with comfortable seating arrangements almost seemed to recreate the grandeur the Mughals were known for.¬†

Coming to the food, we ordered a chicken malai kebab, galouti kebab, daryabadi biryani and mutton chap. The chicken malai kebab arrived first. The chicken was nice, tender and very well marinated. The ¬†cheese and curd used to marinate the chicken balanced the spices beautifully. The galouti kebab was up next and it was simply mind blowing. One of the best I have had in quite a while. They were wonderfully succulent and rich and full of flavors. It was served properly with a side of very well done thin and crisp parathas. I liked the fact that they served the galoutis with the parathas and did not make one order the parathas separately as many places tend to do. The Daryabadi biryani which is one of their signatures was again beautifully done. It was not very rich yet had a brilliant blend of flavorful spices. The mutton and also the rice were cooked to perfection. The mutton chap was also one of the better versions of the very popular dish that i have tasted in a while. We finished off our meal with a shahi tukra and a firni. The shahi tukra was nice with the flavor and color of the saffron coming to the fore.¬†

The service was swift and the staff nice and courteous. The price tag was quite reasonable considering the quality of the food.

Overall we had a delightful experience here and would surely go back for more. Great authentic food, lovely glamorous ambiance and with a reasonable pocket pinch- I mean what more can one ask for?
Enjoy!¬†
Cheers! :)

I don't think I have tried any other chicken dishes - with such good mutton preparations, who needs chicken? :)

I am also a diehard fan of their firni and shahi tukda. Both the desserts are great, and after a biryani, it is a pity that I can only eat any one of them.

I tried their haleem during the season, and it was the best that I have had in Kolkata.

I haven't tried their ¬†Chinese dishes yet. I guess whenever I go to this place, I cannot think beyond the biryanis.

The service at the restaurant is top notch.

The only reason I have dunked half a star is because of their mutton curries - they are good, but not as lipsmacking as the biryanis, and hence they pull the rating down a notch.

2016-07-22 04:33:39
Sayantika Dutta
1340482
4.5
I have no idea, why I had not stepped foot into India Restaurant sooner. It was my very first date with it and I could already find myself swooning at the smell of freshly made Biriyani right when I entered the main seating area. 

Location and Ambience:

Situated right beside Khidderpore, Fancy Market, the restaurant is beautifully set up and is an absolute contrast to the hot and sweltering condition outside. Blocking the traffic, the horns and the heat away, India restaurant has managed to pull together a beautiful ambience for its diners. 

The Food:

While the ambience is beautiful, the service will make you happy, the main thing that pulls you back to this restaurant again and again is definitely the food. We ordered a whole bunch of things and were highly pleased with Almost everything. 

For the first course, we ordred-
- Chicken Chatpata Kebab and
- Mutton galawati kebab

While both the kebabs were exceptionally made, the Galawati had to be the favourite. It came with a huge Lucknawi Paratha on the side and was a sheer delight to eat. I could not have been more pleased. The chicken kebabs were on wings and lived up to their name.

For the main course, we moved onto-
-¬†¬† ¬†Kachi biriyani,
-¬†¬† ¬†Awadhi biryani,
-¬†¬† ¬†Dum ka Murgh
-¬†¬† ¬†Fresh Lime Sodas

The only point of disappointment in the main course was the fresh lime soda, but that was hardly the concern. While the kacchi biriyani was excellent, I have hardly any words to describe the Awadhi. It came out of a freshly dum bhara hua, earthen pot and was the sealed top was released right in front of us. The steam escaping the pot was enough to make me go weak in my knees and my stomach. With renewed energy, we tucked into the second batch of biriyani, accompanied by the beautifully luscious Dum ka Murgh, which could go equally well with a bread.

Yes, we moved onto desserts to. For desserts we ordered-
-¬†¬† ¬†The shahi Tukra and
-¬†¬† ¬†The Firni

The shahi tukra was an absolute disappointment for me. I hardly had more than a spoon of it and quickly settled for the Firni. Oh My God, nothing could have managed to end the meal on a better note than the firni itself.

In case that you are planning to visit this legendary eatery soon, make sure you order the Awadhi biryani, the Galawati kebab and of course the Firni.

2016-07-07 23:50:56
RoySabya
7508191
4.5
India Restaurant is an epitome of fine tasting Biriyani and other Mughlai dishes. It had been in my bucket-list for long and though I savored their Biriyani and Firni through home/office deliveries, but I took the journey to the Kidderpore outlet sometime ago. The best way to go is to look for Fancy Market and then cross it while staying in the opposite side and reach the next traffic signal. And India is on your left side.

The sit-in options have been hugely revamped. Earlier it was in a small room towards the end of the ground floor. But now they have taken up the entire building and remodeled the 1st/2nd and 3rd Floors (I sat on the 2nd floor, so wont know a lot about the ambiance and decor of the other floors). The ambiance is new and fresh, the waiters courteous, the sitting is spacious and soothing.

Once you settle down, you read through the Menu Card which has taken up a makeover as well. Inadvertently, the order had Daryabadi Biriyani (they hail from Daryagunj in Lucknow and hence the name Daryabadi), Galauti Kabab, Kakori Kabab and Firni. The kebabs were perhaps the best I have had in Kolkata. I mean after tasting kababs at Peshawri (ITC Sonar Kolkata) and Oudh 1590 (Deshapriya Park), the ones from India were smooth and the best in a long long time. The unmistakable biriyani was next and its taste was the most impressive of its contemporaries (the Arsalans, Shirazs and the Aminias). Last but not the least the Firni was mind blowing too and it was a perfect ending to a sumptuous meal.

Overall a big thumbs up to the owners for exposing Kolkatans to this paradise of Mughlai cuisine - India Restaurant.

##

2016-07-06 19:50:43
Ammeet Dutta
273422
4.0
My maiden visit to this joint was motivated by outstanding reviews on Zomato by my fellow foodies.And truth be told, i was floored by the ambience,staff behaviour,decor,hygiene and the food of course.
Visited the joint yesterday in the early afternoon . The first floor dining area was almost empty with just a couple of diners at a faraway corner.Was attended to immediately by the courteous staff.
Ordered the mutton kacchi biryani,chicken biryani and chicken tawa.Firstly the mutton kacchi biryani was quite different as compared to the traditional biryani that we have ¬†in Kolkata.The difference is that in kacchi biryani raw(kacchi) meat is cooked together with the rice. Thus the name kacchi biryani.In case of traditional(pakki) biryani the meat is cooked separately and then mixed in the rice.This birynai is more famous in Dhaka and is slightly more wet and spicier as compared to pakki biryani. I liked it immensely.Quantity is huge with a large fleshy piece ¬†of mutton,gigantic piece of potato and boiled egg.The chicken biryani was also very good with right amount of moistness and spices.Quality of rice used was also top-notch.
The tawa chicken comprised of six medium sized cubes of boneless chicken in a thick yellowish gravy garnished with slices of onion,tomato an capsicum.Slightly on the oilier side as expected in a Mughlai joint.
Prices are reasonable and inclusive of all taxes.Thus no complex calculations and brainstorming on the rationale of various taxes levied on dining out.:) Cheers!!!! H

For the ambience five out of five. India Restaurant who is known for his North Indian Cuisines didn't disappoint me at all. The Service was outstanding, within 10 minutes the food was served. Now coming to the food, we ordered 2 chicken biryanis and 2 mutton biryanis, chicken cheese kebab, firni and shahi tukra. The biryani was one of the tastiest biryanis I ever tasted. The chicken was juicy and soft, on the other hand the potato was well cooked. Now coming to the kebabs, this cheese kebabs was probably the best kebabs I ever had. Now coming to the deserts the firni and the shahi tukra both were quite similar in taste but honestly they snatched more 0.5 ratings from me otherwise I was thinking to settle at 4. So for me its 4.5 Stars and they deserve this. And a big thank you to Zomato for their valuable food menu suggestions.

2016-05-23 09:17:29
Devraj Lahiri
6916171
5.0
And when the mind gets numbed by the allure of the Hooghly, quench your soul with the aroma of the Awadhi Biriyani. And possibly eat it too. Let your pilgrimage end at India restaurant. A byword for ecstacy, India like it's namesake, is a microcosm of the social fabric, it so proudly exists in. And boy, what joy to be a part of its culinary experience. The India biriyani, as I have fondly been calling it for years now, is a dry preparation. The hint of oil is minimal and the spice is markedly higher. So if one is looking for solace, simply tuck into their range of biriyanis. It would be a blasphemy on my part to even rate and compare them. Gluttony is a ritual for me and I would rather stick to it. Do not forget to add a rezala or a korma to the meal, though puritans prefer to have their biriyani separately. For me the concept of 'bhaat-dal' extends here too. The tandoori murg is another delicacy, one should never miss. They come in two and four pieces for half and full plates, respectively. And is a killer. End your meal with the ethereal firni or shahi tukda. Happy, go back to the Hooghly. The river will look alluring. More so now. With India in your guts.
They make Chinese too, but have never been able to go beyond the tandoori and the biriyani.
If you are still waiting to be amazed, hop on to a conveyance and travel over to Khiderpore. Come back a satisfied soul.

2016-02-03 15:14:18
Arghya Deep
10852711
4.0
Note: The meal was a complimentary one from the restaurant for the Zomato meetup.

India Restaurant, Khidderpore had been on my bookmarks for quite a long time. Having heard numerous praises from zomans about its biryanis it was only a matter of time that I would pay a visit.However it came as a pleasant surprise when one fine morning I found a mail from zomato about a meetup whose venue was to be India restaurant! yay!Wow, I'd be meeting fellow foodies too! Next was what to expect from India Restaurant. They serve awesome biryanis. But then again I found out that they had recently renovated their upper floors & looking forward to introduce new menu.
So upon visiting the place you find this restaurant which resembles most other eateries of yesteryears of kolkata. Seating arrangement is cramped & it feels you are in yet another cabin-styled eating house.Then you notice the entrance to the upper floors.
The doorman opens the gate & voila! Its a completely different scenario from what you were seeing until now!The gold- yellow colour & lighting scheme along with the carefully chosen chairs & sofas give you that royal mughal feeling. They even use golden mats on the table in place of boring laminated papers.Of course I was impressed. This definitely was different from those regular outlets decorated with glass top tables or coffee coloured sofas!
The first floor also has a nice waiting lounge for about 12-15 people. Great place to take selfies & checking in on zomato.
I got introduced to Mr. Vicky Chen, the manager who would be our host for the lunch.
Now to the food.
From the mocktails menu I ordered Virgin Mary, Shirley temple & Grappa. Let me be honest Bloody Mary without alcohol is just tomato juice & very disappointing.The second one was citrus & apple based & tasted good. But the grappa was mind blowing. Of course a tall glass filled with grape juice, syrup & topped up with vanila ice cream can hardly go wrong. But still all of us had liked it very much & each had ordered at least one of it. However note that the mocktails weren't part of the standard menu, & you may not find them right now. However they plan to introduce the new menu shortly.
Coming to the starters, we had Thai sashlik, Paneer kurkure, Pineapple tandoori in the veg. offering & Chicken cheese kebab, Chicken malai kebab & Fish Sarsonwali in the non-veg.
The Thai sashlik was good, nothing extra ordinary, the paneer kurkure was good, but the pineapple tandoori was definitely the best in the lot. It was chicken tandoori without the chicken. So all the vegetarians out there can find out what they are missing out by not having chicken tandoori ;).
Now of course it was the time for the stars of the day, biryanis India Restaurant is known for. We had Daryabadi kacchhi Biryani, Awadhi biryani along with regular Chicken & Mutton Biryani in the menu while the vegetarian people had the choice of veg. biryani or Peas Pulao in the rice. Once we jumped into the biryanis we knew why they are known as among the best in Kolkata. The rice was well cooked & flavoured. The Daryabadi biryani is served in a sealed clay handi. As the rice is cooked along with raw pieces of meat, the flavour is infused in the rice as well. The Awadhi biryani is cooked with vegetables and is spicier than the regular biryani, but taste is in a different league altogether. The chicken & mutton pieces were adequately marinated, soft & juicy. Overall the Biryanis were surely among the finest in Kolkata.
Also in the menu was choice of various naans & rotis of which I tried the kesaria & butter ones. The butter naan was of regular taste, but this is the first time I tried Kesariya Naan. It has a much sweet note to it, which may not appeal to everyones' tastebuds. but matched with the right spicy side-dish, it can win hands down.
From the side dish I tried Mutton Dakbangla, Mutton Ra-Ra Punjabi & Chicken Afghani. The mutton dishes seemed fine, while I found the Chicken one better. The dal fry & Aloo dum too were rightly cooked as I heard from the others.
I also tasted their various raitas which were as accompaniments. The boondi & mix raitas were of standard taste, while I found the pineapple raita to stand out. definitely this restaurant knows how to prepare their pineapples :D
In the dessert menu they had Firni, Shahi Tukda & Gajar ka halwa, of which I tried all. No points for guessing I am a sweet loving bengali :P. The Firni was a bit tad sweeter than one would expect, while the shahi tukda was a bit grainy from inside. The gajar ka halwa was a bit overcooked & smelled a bit burnt. On asking they served a second plate which was better.
Overall the experience was memorable. The staff were courteous, the dishes much decorated & prepared with care. However I am not sure how much this was due to the 'Zomato meetup' tag. Hope to find their service as good when I visit them the next time.
Thanks Zomato & India Restaurant for having us. Will wait for the next time ;)
Till then, happy eating.

2016-02-03 15:05:06
Sumit Surai
11641
4.0
When I ate here last, during my college days, it was a small, single floor restaurant. On my last visit to Kidderpore, I noticed they have expanded and have added two floors above the old one. I made a note then to come back soon to check out the new section. So, when I received an invitation from Zomato last week for a food meet-up here, I was more than happy.

Ambiance

I was expecting great interiors, bit nothing like what I saw. It was grand. I was not expecting something like this here in Kidderpore. Perfect place for a family dine out or a date. Selection of music was good and so was the volume. Not too loud, nor too soft. I would personally suggest them to play Arabic string instrumental tracks. Will go perfectly with the decor and their specialty food.

Service

Excellent. Quick, attentive and friendly. Mr. Vicky Chen, the manager, and his team, made their best efforts and I must say I was impressed.

Food

Now the main thing. Food. Most of the items we tried were not from their regular menu. We were told they are trying to incorporate these in the regular menu by the end of February.

The mocktails were refreshing. I tried Deep Blue Sea and Grappa. While Grappa (grape based with ice cream topping) had the best look, Deep Blue Sea was better taste-wise.

Among the starters, the veg ones, surprisingly, won hearts. While the Paneer Kurkure had a great texture and tasted good too, it was the Pineapple Tandoori that unanimously was voted the queen among the starters.

The Mixed Shashlik didn't score for me. I didn't like the fried covering. For me the best among non-veg starters was Fish Sarsonwali. Fat fish fillet and spicy. The Chicken Malai Kebab was good too with soft pieces of chicken. The Chicken Cheese Kebab was a bit dry and hard when they first served it. Once complained they cooked a second batch, which was far better. But I personally am not a fan of Cheese Kebabs as I like my kebabs more spicy. If you are a cheese kebab fan, you would like it.

For breads they served a variety of naans. Butter naan, Kesaria naan and Kabuli naan. I loved them all. Soft and delicious. Perfect to wrap around the variety of gravies they served. I tried the Mutton Ra-Ra-Punjabi, Mutton Dakbangla and Chicken Afghani. The gravies were rich and tasty. The mutton was soft and juicy and the julienned chicken was well cooked and not dry.

Among the veg dishes, the Kashmiri Aloo Dum looked the best, but the meat dishes were so good, I didn't have room for it. The naans were excellent, and I wanted to have another helping, but restrained myself as we were still waiting for the biryanis to be served, which is the USP of this place.

The Kachchi biryani had alubookhara in it, which gave it an unique taste. A bit on the sweeter side, I think this is a must try for Biryani lovers, as the taste is different from the regular ones. But I found the Awadhi Biryani, served in a handi, the best. The mutton pieces again were excellent. If you are a biryani lover, you just can't miss visiting this place.

For desserts there were Gajar Ka Halwa, Sahi Tukra and Firni. Going by the ambiance of the new section, they have ample scope of improvement as far as plating of the desserts are concerned. It will only add feathers to their cap. Taste-wise I liked the gajar ka halwa and the sahi tukra. But the firni was a tad sweet for me. Personally I like a less sweet firni. But if you like yours sweeter, you will love it.

The overall experience was great and I am looking forward to coming back here once the new items are added to their regular menu.

2016-02-02 15:50:54
Pawan Jaiswal/The Food Crave
73744
4.0
LOCATION AND DESCRIPTION: Well, It was a Zomato meet up at this venue Named India Restaurant located at khidirpore market. All thanks to our CM for choosing this place and letting us know that there is something like this place still exists in Kolkata. A very old and renowned place Known for their Brilliant biriyani for years. If you want to see a mini Dubai this is the place for you. From the classy ambiance to Waiters to the entire hospitality. As i heard about this place was something else and i get a shocker when i entered the place.

AMBIANCE AND STAFF: The ambiance is huge. Divided in three parts starting from the ground floor which is open moving towards 1st floor which is made of Silver interiors and very classy indeed following the best part of the building the second floor. Which was of Golden, yellow with eye warming interiors and simply made me felt like i am at dubai for a moment. Dining in here gives you a royal feel with the glitters of the place. Resto is quite huge with lots of tables up for grabs in forms of tables as well as sofas. Its clean and run in full A.c.. Staff here simply the nicest, attends to you properly, listens to you with ears open and are very polite. Till the best group of staff i have met till now.
Everything was very well managed by the floor manager Mr. Vikki Chen, a special thanks to him for taking care of everything with such calm way.

FOOD: So here we are finally for the main part. Basically when we visit a resto we often don't have a chance to taste everything. But this place offered almost everything of their specialty all thanks to Team Zomato for such a huge list.

We Dined in and began with the Mocktails in forms of Shirley Temple as a beginner followed by Deep blue sea and Grappa.

Shirley Temple tasted a mix of Orange and flavours of other fruits which i couldn't guess. thou it contained more a tangy taste which was simply nice.

Deep blue Sea was also very good, It looked proper with the decoration and the taste was even better.

Grappa was a huge one. The taste of grapes in a drink, what more you need. Filled with ice cream on the top and the look of the drink was pleasant as well.

Next we went down to the Starters which contained both Veg and Non Veg.

Beginning with Pineapple Tandoori, Paneer Kurkure followed with Chicken Malai Kebab, Chicken Cheese Kebab and Fish Sarsowali.

Pineapple Tandoori is a must try here even if you are a diehard N-V. I think it should be their trademark starter. A fruit turned and reflected into a tandoor was a surprise for me. Smelling and eating it out gave me the feeling of eating like Tandoori chicken with flavour of Pineapple.

Paneer Kurkure was also on a satisfactory note.

Chicken Malai Kebab was very nice. It was contained in a stick with different vegetable. Fried well and was equally hot when served.

Chicken Cheese Kebab was good. Chicken marinated and roasted with cheese stuffing in it. thou few of my fellow friends found it difficult to break thou i didn't find one. And when they served it again it was even softer to me.

Fish Sarsonwali Looked like Reshmi Kebab, but when broken you find good amount of fish in it. Thou a bit dry inside still i believe kebab has to get dry after being fried in such a heat. taste was very spicy and according to me it was the best in N-V starters.

We dropped down to the main course where lots of things were in queue. To be honest i had tried the entire N-V section but didn't tried the Veg at all as was bit ill :-p. Served on the table were Chicken and Mutton Biriyani, Kacchi Biriyani and Awadhi Biriyani followed by Chicken Afgani, Mutton Ra-Ra Punjabi and Mutton Dakbangla for the side dish. Lastly we had the Butter Nan, Kesariya Nan with three forms of Raita and three forms of Desserts in form of Firni, Shahi Tukra and Gajar Halwa.

Both the Mutton and Chicken Biriyani were excellent. Simply what we call a biriyani. Pieces were also satisfactory, the potato was done justice and was soft indeed.

Kacchi Biriyani was tasting different from the normal ones. It has other form of spices which kept me reminding of Hyderabadi biriyani.

Awadhi Biriyani was even better. It came in a Handi decorated pretty well.¬†

Chicken Afgani seemed very ordinary to me. it looked eating like Reshmi butter masala.

Mutton Ra-Ra Punjabi was a good pick. Taste was brilliant. the mutton was breaking easily and was very juicy inside.

Mutton Dakbangla was just different like its name. It contained taste of Mutton chaap and Mutton Masala together. A combined taste i felt, don't know about others. Again mutton was made well and breaking easily.

Butter nan was good so was the Kesariya nan. It was thick and breaking easily and was equally soft.

Coming to the end of the table so i must say i was bit disappointed with the Desserts.¬†

Firni was pretty ordinary, Shahi tukra was not upto the mark and gajar halwa could have been much better than this. A huge improvement is required in this section, specially to the decoration section of the desserts.

QNQ AND PRICES: Quality of all the food served were no doubt very good. Impressed with the quality and the quantity as well. Prices are fine and reasonable.

CONCLUSION: All thanks to Team zomato and our CM for such a nice lunch and selection of place. And later a return gift as well to the same place made it even better. Will be surely moving to this place again in some time to try the left outs.
Well i wish all the luck to them. Cheers

NOTE: the review is based on my personal visit and Experience to this place.

If you are a fan of mughal cuisines or you love that Royal feeling while eating or else lets put it this way that you always want to visit a new place totally different from the regular restaurant's , then I must tell you my friend that my recommendation and choice is
INDIA RESTAURANT as you won't be dissapointed with the fine experience .

Let me give every crisp bit of detail about my thorough experience about this place , so at first let me disclose the main part that on 30/1/2016 a group of foodies from Kolkata were invited for a Zomato meet up at this luxurious and royal ambiance based restaurant to taste and indulge in a wide table spread of mughal cuisines as well as other varieties that their restaurant offers .

AMBIANCE & HOSPITALITY --

The restaurant is divided in two floors which are non ac that is in the ground floor and the ac one which is on the 1 st floor so we headed to the ac seating area and as we were a group of 10 to 12 people so slowly we settled down in our royal tables with fine cutleries on our table welcoming us and within a few minutes servers came and helped us with serving water in our glasses and while all this was happening i took some time to get into the mood of eating as the whole set up and decoration of the place just got me mesmerised and without any delay I ended up clicking a lot pictures of the lights around the whole area , then i captured a few shots of the ceilings which were beautifully done and then had my eyes on the chairs and tables which were crafted very much like the feel of some mughal emperor's time which is highly commendable to see in a restaurant in Kolkata .
The whole section is fully done up nice and bright with colours of gold ,yellow ,white ,chocolate brown and black combination for sofas and also the marbles floors all were designer which added a heavy vivid experience setting the mood just so right .

Now let me tell you about the hospitality and service of the waiters, servers and in charge head of our table, that they were absolutely so ready to help you and make you feel comfortable really is a very positive thing in this restaurant making you eat with comfort and care is a rare thing these days.
Then i visited the washroom in between and noticed a house keeping staff is employed outside the washroom who was pretty alert with his job so that's a good thing and for sure coming to the main man behind all this as well as responsible for the whole restaurant of both the floors was the manager Mr Vicky Chen who is really a wonderful and cooperative person as he took great care and gave instructions to the staff in such a manner that it was commendable seeing how the whole unit works with so much passion and hard work .

FOOD & BEVERAGES --

I had started my day with a few mocktails which were SHIRLEYS TEMPLE ,DEEP BLUE and GRAPPA ,now all three drinks differ from each other as in from taste to the presentation as well as colour .
Shirleys temple has a strong taste of orange flavour in it and looks peach in colour then the deep blue sea tastes very much lemon and has blue colour look and finally grappa tastes likes grapes and the colour is also purple and has a ice cream to the topping of it .
All of them are good in their own way however for me deep blue sea and Shirley's temple stood out .

Then we shifted to the starters which were from the veg kitchen first and they were PINEAPPLE TANDOORI ,PANEER STARTERS.
Now the pineapple tandoori was really very nice and the flavour of tandoor was nicely enriched giving my taste buds a good feel as compared to the other paneer and veggie starters listed in the menu that I tried.
Then for non veg starters I had CHICKEN CHEESE KEBAB ,CHICKEN MALAI KEBAB AND FISH SARSONWALI of which let me tell you the best I found was Chicken malai kebab as it was tasting very juicy and the spice was set nicely ,also the meat was soft and easy to chew whereas chicken cheese kebab wasn't bad but little improvement can be done in terms of the meat to be a bit soften and finally the fish sarsonwali was tasting very yummy however a bit dryness was not letting me complete my satisfaction on that one .

So after the end of starters ,now let's come in for the big ones which is the main course ones first veg selection like NAAN,KESARIA NAAN,DAL FRY,KASHMIRI ALOO DAM,SABR-E-BAHAR
and non veg selection like CHICKEN BIRYANI ,MUTTON BIRYANI,KACCHI BIRYANI , AWADHI BIRYANI,MUTTON RA-RA PUNJABI ,MUTTON DAKBANGLA AND CHICKEN AFGHANI .
The veg based dal fry was made very tasty and thick which really goes well with naan and other Roti's ,then the kashmiri aloo was soft as possible and flavoured very nice probably little sweetness was added as the aloo tasted sweet too and the Sabr e bahar was a mix of a lot of vegatables in green curry including paneer too .
The naan ,kesaria naan both were made very soft and not burnt as well as sufficient enough for a proper meal ,coming to the non veg part the Chicken Afghani was a real delight to taste with the meat perfectly made with a lovely aroma of spices and so tender to eat , then the mutton ra ra was a dark colour mutton gravy curry high on taste and some big pieces are in it making it taste yum ,moving on to mutton dakbangla it was pretty much similar however the colour of the gravy was slightly different and the meat was softer in every bite I took .
Now about the biryanis well the mutton and chicken biryani were very good with proper pieces of meat ,egg and aloo spiced up ingredients and the quantity was very much likeable , then the kacchi biryani has a Hyderabadi taste to it and tastes a bit different from the rest but the biryani which stole my heart from this restaurant was the AWADHI HANDI BIRYANI which is like the hallmark of INDIAN CUISINE AND BRINGS A MUGHAL LEGACY in your table when you eat this lovely handi biryani you won't like to eat any other biryani then after as its full in quantity with special top most fine basmati rice,eggs ,mutton and aloos made fully with a total different set of ingredients as its a special dish and surely it does justice in the menu card 100 percent .

Finally after eating this delightful meal with a huge spread we ended our day with some desserts like firni ,shahi tukra and halwa out of which only the firni was rocking but the presentation can be improved ,same goes for the shahi tukra but it was made a little better than the halwa as the halwa did not taste up to the mark however eatable .

Hence a beautiful meet organised by

ZOMATO ( complementary) at INDIA RESTAURANT came to an end as it was very memorable and a beautiful experience altogether .

This place is another hidden treasure discovery from Zomato.

Now lets come to my experience.I visited there on 1st january.
Ambiance:it's a beautiful ¬†two storied place.The glass decoration,cosy sofas and lots of open space have made it comfortable.And specilly the view of hanging various kinds of kebabs in kitchen is an eye soothing view.
Food:We took chicken malai kebab in starter.It was nice.For main course we ¬†tried butter tandoori,chicken butter masala and their special mutton biryani.Butter tandoori was moderate and soft enough.but the chicken butter masala was brilliant.And the biryani,it was amazing.Special mutton biryani comes with two pieces of mutton and one egg.Mutton was very tender and tasty.Their biryani is even better then Arsalan and aminiya Biryani.But i took away their plain mutton biryani for home,it was not upto the mark.So its better to try their special biryani.

And they did not offer us mouri and mishri too.Otherwise it was fine.service was prompt.The security guards were very cordial and they were suggesting us better places in the restaurant for taking selfies.

Price:A little bit overpriced than usual biryani place.But the place is worth of it.For three people cost was approxly 900.
But the overall dining experience was satisfactory and demand a revisit.Thank you zomato for suggesting such a nice place.

2015-12-23 12:22:08
Rio Gupta
319096
4.0
Visited India restaurant on 22/12/2015 for a dinner with friends. Went in at 9.30 pm it was almost full. We sat in the first floor, when we entered the place the first thing to be noticed was the nice decor (nicely done interiors) thumbs up for that.
We ordered chicken special biriyani, Galouti kabab (winter special) , Chicken Bharta ,lucknowi paratha, sweet fresh lime sodas.
Biriyani was very nice and i would admit that it was better than arsalan's in terms of quality it had two pieces of chicken one boiled egg and our famous boiled "aalu" :)
Galouti Kabab was also very good it melts in the mouth, i've had better galouti kababs in the past but still it was good.
The paratha was very big in size it was ok.
The only complain is with the Chicken Bharta, The chicken pieces were very hard as if frozen chicken was used in cooking & the pieces were tasting like either not fresh or not properly washed before cooking, also there was supposed to be more gravy but instead it was floating in oil.
Service was super fast and nice no complaints with that.
Management please look into this and make sure whatever you cook the chicken pieces are soft.

Overall the food quality was good and light or rather i would say better than Arsalan, a very nice experience. Although this place is far away from where i stay but would try to visit more often.
Cheers
RG

To me, India Restaurant is a legend and I would go back every now and then to this place for a great meal.

2015-07-13 22:28:39
Epicurious Madhuja
643805
3.0
Located near Fancy Market in Khidderpore, I chose this place for a casual family dinner solely based on the rave reviews of the food. One doesn't come to such places expecting a nice ambiance or an overall fine experience, but simply to satisfy taste buds. But that is what left me disappointed on several counts. First, there was nothing very 'reshmi' about the chicken reshmi kabab... It tasted very average and the meat was neither soft nor juicy. Next, the mutton rezala though quite nice in taste was a dampener owing to the cuts of meat used. It was 70% fat and 30% meat.    The excess thick fat was not just a waste but also killed the fine flavors of the rezala gravy. As the Kachhi biryani (specialty) was over, we opted for their regular mutton biryani which was done quite nicely and lived up to our expectation. Except in one matter: once again, the quality and cut of meat was way too fatty to be either tasteful or enjoyable. Maybe it was the wrong time to try this place: the last weekend of the month of Ramadan when the crowds are at their peak. The only saving grace of the evening was the cheese-wrapped chicken kabab. The thick coating of molten tandoor-grilled cheese blended really well with the chicken, leading to an overall amazing combination. If I would go back to this place, it would be only for this one item they offer.

We wanted to visit this restaurant for a long time, finally yesterday we made it happen. Yes! it is one of the best biriyani destination in kolkata and surrounding suburbans. So, you can guess the craze of this place.

Staff were polite and helpful, service was prompt.

Coming to the food, we ordered special mutton biriyani, special chicken biriyani, Chicken malai kebab, mutton rezalla, green salad (as raita was not available then), phirni and sahi tukra.

Special Biriyani consists of two large pieces of chicken/mutton, one potato and one boiled egg. The rice was perfectly cooked long grains, perfect proportion of spices and quantity was more than enough for a single person. The chicken/mutton was tender but a little dry inside, wish it would little juicier inside (like arsalan).

Chicken malai kebab was also very good, soft and tasty comes with pudina chutney and shredded onions. One plate consists 6 pieces of chicken.

The mutton rezalla was the best dish we had here. It was awesome. I still feel the taste and flavour when i'm writing this. Really! Super soft, super buttery, super flavoured mutton piece comes with similarly delicious gravy, surely you will not let it go without licking the plate.

Phirni was not bad but there is nothing special than other restaurants.

The Sahi tukra was also good. But I would prefer it from oudh1590.

Anyways overall I loved the restaurant and will come back shortly to try their Dariyabadi biriyani and mutton barah kebab.

Its a gem of a place, folks.

Its a very good place in the city for people who love their meat. Towards the end the waiters were also I surprised seeing us eat so much of meat :D

2015-02-21 13:46:12
Ruchismita Mukherjee
444517
4.0
If you are a true Biryani lover, you would know that nothing can fulfill a biryani craving other than a good, juicy plate of biryani. Also you would know that there is hardly anything in the world that a generous plate of biryani cannot cure! So it is that kind of biryani we are talking about here...
I have not been to India Restaurant, but I had heard so much about them that I decided to attend a Biryani festival they were participating in (in Eco Space, New Town, and thanks to that because it is tough for people up east to travel all the way to Kidderpore to grab a taste of heavenly biryani). And boy, was I in for a surprise!
I tried their paratha with mutton chaap, and chicken bharta, and to top it all the ever-so-good Kacchhi Biryani. 
This was like the marriage of the true-bred Awadhi Dastarkhwan and the Sub-e-Bangal Moghlai fare.
Words cannot describe the amazing experience that I had. Each grain of rice glistened with moist ghee, intact in size and texture, yet melted in the mouth. The mutton was tender and rightly flavored, handpicked, juicy pieces - lean yet meaty, soft yet striated! The boiled egg and potato was part of the package which made all bengalis go weak in the knees! The potato, once I dug into it felt like a lump of pure butter - dum-pukht or cooked over a 'slow flame'...and that made all the difference! I am told that the Daryabadi Biryani is also a must try...
The place is pocket-friendly, and service very prompt. Very, very earnestly and highly recommended by me.
Who knows maybe this Biryani will even cure a heartbreak!

2015-02-16 03:00:43
Goutam Mahapatro
4479791
4.0
I was in kolkata a few days back to meet some friends. We all wanted to have a decent meal and then we found this place while surfing on zomato. It was easy to locate this place. It is located beside fancy market in kidderpore. India Restaurant is one among the best biriyani and kebab restaurants in kolkata. We reached this place around 1:30pm and it was crowded. They have air conditioned dining rooms and also the non ac dining rooms. We preferred the ac one. Here the service is a bit disappointing. After we sat down the waiter took about 5 minutes to address us. We asked for some water first and then ordered our food. 

For starters we ordered chicken tikka kebab, chicken afgani and chicken hot n sour soup. The starters were at our table in around 10 minutes. The kebabs were exceptional. They were tender, juicy and were perfectly cooked. I loved the chicken afgani. It was an amazing experience for my palate. The soup was fine.

For the main course we had a daryabadi biryani, laccha paratha, rumali roti, mutton chap and chicken dopiyaza. The mutton chap and the chicken dopiyaza were very oily. We had to drain out the oil first and then eat. I liked both the items. The were properly done and the meat was also cooked well. The laccha paratha and the rumali roti were spot on. The biryani was delecious. The mutton pieces were cooked to perfection. 

Then for deserts we ordered firni and sahi tukra. The sahi tukra was a royal treat to the taste buds. It had a nice flavour of saffron and cardamom. The firni was equally good. I had a lovely time here. This place serves some amazing food at reasonable prices and I recommend every one to try out this place.

2014-10-17 10:34:26
Budhaditya Bose
147900
3.0
One of kolkata's most famous restaurants for 'Biryani'. Situated in the heart of khiddirpore, the place is deemed to serve a good mughlai affair.¬†
Ambience has been modernized recently as is evident from the interiors, but place is still small with lot more number of tables than there should be.
Has an A/C separate area which is an added advantage.¬†
Lets get down to the food now, on a weekday afternoon at 3pm the restaurant was bustling with people. Commendable i must say, cause looking at the prices it was sure that the crowd was here for GOOD FOOD and not pocket-friendly food.
We ordered - Chicken biryani (Yes, I and my friend dont prefer the mutton), Mutton chaap, Chicken butter masala and FIrni.

Chicken biryani - was good. well cooked. rightly flavoured. Nothing heavenly.
Mutton chaap - Over cooked, meat was chewy and the chaap gravy had more oil than the masala.
Chicken butter masala - white in colour! First time in my life a waiter tells me butter masala is supposed to be white and malai butter masala is supposed to be red. Anyways at Rs.180 for 4 medium chunks of chicken is pretty expensive. The chicken was over cooked and hard. And the gravy was more oil than masala.
Firni - the saviour of the day. Was beautifully made.

Overall experience. Is ok for a one time visit. But definitely not if you want to showcase calcutta biryani to your friends.

##

2014-10-05 13:11:50
Sucharita
861173
4.0
India Restaurant is not the most sanitary of restaurants what with the perennially unclean tables, glasses, rickety chairs and littered floors but if you rise above that and listen to your hunger-struck bodies, this is the place to be! The air-conditioned section charges about 30-50 bucks more per dish than the ordinary section, as is the case with most such restaurants.¬†

My father had heard of the place from Pakistani co-passengers on a train and we had to come here, as ashamed as we were not having known about it ourselves!

It was my brother's treat and we ordered:
(1) Chicken Hariyali Kebab: Six large chunks of succulent chicken that is bound to leave you wishing you could have the whole plate to yourself! To top it off, they do provide adequate amounts of onion and chutney to go with the chicken.
(2) Chicken Reshmi Kabab: Squirt enough lemon juice on your kebabs and you will be transported to other worlds! Tasty, juicy and large-sized, the kebabs are served hot.¬†
(3) Mutton Biryani: Delicious, with one tender piece of mutton and one well-cooked potato; and just the right amount of oil, neither too much nor too less.
(4) Chicken Special Biryani: The only thing special about Special Biryani is the extra piece of chicken (and an egg). Upon later reflection, we agreed that it would have been better to take TWO plates of their ordinary chicken biryani rather than the special one. It was lip-smacking delicious but the potato will remain the star for me. The rice is white and orange in parts, something I don't prefer to see but it didn't harm the taste itself. ¬†
(5) Mutton Rezala: A bit too sweet for my liking and lacking a bit of spice, I enjoyed dipping ends of my Tandoori Roti in the gravy and munching away. However, my father sure made a clean job of it.
(6) Chicken Chap: It was rich, red and ripping good.¬†
(7) Tandoori Roti: Ordinary and easily turned cold, dry and difficult to tear.
(8) Phirni: Only for those with a sweet tooth. If I were to close my eyes and eat it, I would have believed you if you told me it was mishti doi, only denser.

Service was swift and friendly.¬†Amounting to a touch above Rs 1300, we paid the bill and left the place content and willing to return as soon as possible.

They have 2 different sections -AC and non AC sections.. There's nothing to tell about ambiance as it is nothing special..So coming to the food directly.. We ordered India Special Cheese Kabab, Daryabadi biriyani ,one special mutton biriyani and Chicken Achari..

Cooked very lightly , the chicken was soft and juicy surrounded by a thick cheesy layer and grilled from outside..I would definitely visit again for the kababs at least.. Cant say about other kababs but this, being their special kabab is likely to compete some of the great Moghlai restaurants in the city..
Coming to the biriyani--Darybabadi biriyani was very light , contained 2 pieces of mutton ,1 egg and a large potato. Mutton was boiled and cooked perfectly and they serve generous quantity.. This tasted great along with the chicken achari which was recommended by the servers..Its a boneless dish ..The gravy was just brilliant but the chicken was a great disappointment .. Those were not boiled perfectly and we had to chew and chew and chew and finally had to get rid of them..
If u r hovering through that area, u might take a chance to taste their biriyani and kababs.. Well recommended!!!

2014-02-02 22:42:16
Poorna Banerjee
2686
4.5
This review is actually written after two days of Kabab eating from India hotel Kidderpore stall at City Center I at the Biryani Kabab festival. The manager assured me that all the kababs they had there were also available at the restaurant. I went there yesterday and got the Chicken Cheese Kabab, which took 15 minutes to cook, and was served with a side of salad and mint chutney. The cheese formed a thick crust around the meat, and squeezing some lemon on it cut through the thick cheese and gave it a lovely balance. It was also super-heavy. 

My friend got a Mutton Handi which was quite good, and we also split a Chicken Peshawari Kabab today. The Peshawari Kabab is a bunch of chicken wings coated in a curd-based marinade cooked in tandoor. I loved dipping it into the mint chutney and eating it with some raw onions. It was also quite heavy, and I was full after eating a plate of it. There was also the Kachhi Biryani which I wanted to pack home, but it was wiped clean by the time I ordered it. Would love to go to the hotel soon and get me some more kababs and Biryani.

For the experience of Day One, check this link - http://presentedbyp.blogspot.in/2014/02/biryani-kabab-festival-at-city-center-i.html



----- 17 May, 2013 -----

Two Words - Daryabadi Biryani. If you are around Fancy Market area, and you want to eat Biryani with dry fruits, especially Aloo bukhara in it, then this is the place. One plate is BIG for one person, and even a big eater like me cannot finish it all without struggling. We generally order one Daryabadi Biryani, a mutton/chicken Chaap, and a chicken hariyali tikka for two people, and that is happiness within 500/-, and a full stomach for two. If you are lucky, you will also get the shahi tukda, which drips with clotted cream.

Service is brisk, and very efficient. You should see the way they carry food around, almost about to topple, but then suddenly they manage not to topple at all. The skill is worth watching. I have been here a number of times, although not in the last year. I have heard their standard have fallen slightly, but I will not believe it until I eat their meat again.

##

2013-07-10 09:54:31
Sayak Kundu
389585
4.0
Memories flood back as I decided to write my review for India but then I decided to have a go at India once before I would start to write this so that I could state the present situation of the restaurant also.
Then I got busy with my life and I forgot until life sprang up a surprise for me.
I got selected in G.R.S.E. to complete my internship and of course going to Metiabruz from my house would have to be via Khidderpore.
However again every day I used to see it and every day I would think, not today, I will be here for 2 months non stop anyways.
It all boiled down to the last 2 days of my internship.

On the second last day I went and decided to sit and eat so I ordered a Mutton Biryani, Chicken chaap and then a paratha.
The biryani was very less spicy and low on oil. It is good isn't it?? If you can keep a biryani which tastes like a biryani with less spices and oil it is advantageous what matters is the taste and it was right there just on the mark. Not the best biryani because you just can't compare some of the leading ones today as all are more or less around the same mark. Some a bit less some a bit more.

The chicken chaap gravy was really fine and when I asked for more masala and less oil I was served to my liking which is what I appreciate. In a fast running Mughlai joint if someone takes out time to bring the order just like you wanted you can't help but appreciate it. Too small thing to appreciate? No, it really does make a difference as very few pay attention or care enough. However sadly I could not enjoy the chaap It had a burnt smell in it. 

Must have been a mistake but I feel the management could maybe keep an eye on whether the curry is all right. If it is not good enough then take the chaap off the menu for the time being and start making the base gravy or whatever that can be called again. Trust me if anybody can then India can surely. It is the single most well known restaurant in whole of Khidderpore thus of course they have done very well as the are is where Muslim is a majority and thus serving the cuisine which matches the preferences of the crowd surely does well. This can also be seen through the fact that despite bengali cuisine is a household regularity people still go to so many bengali restaurants. Its nearness to Fancy Market has also been an advantage as many people come here for different reasons. For me it was always some pirated game DVD's :P and thus India was my choice for a lunch.

The Paratha was very good but oily as I tried to reduce the oil by pressing it with a napkin but I wished there were some other breads available then.
The last day of my internship I packed a Daryabadi Biryani back home. Now the daryabadi biryani is rich and a bit sweet because a lot of raisins nuts and other fruits do into it and numerous spices. The briyani here is too rich and oily and different quite a lot from it's regular biryani though pretty good to taste. The mutton pieces were 2 in number. While one of them was perfectly cooked and soft and melt in the mouth type the other was rather a bit chewy. However the new taste and touch to the regular biryani will be something you will remember.

The decor is nice especially in the A.C. section with tiled walls and marbled floors, white ceiling. Quite nice for a regular Mughlai halt in fact quite better than the regular mughlai halt I should say.

I will miss it again for God knows how many days till I can pay another visit. The fact that the area is too crowded and car parking there is tough is also a disadvantage.

Despitr the chaap with a burnt taste and the slightly chewy piece of mutton in the daryabadi biryani I am still giving it a 4 based on old memories and the fact that they have been more or less always right on their taste thing.

2013-07-03 21:02:32
Amit Pal
12924
3.0
Went to the restaurant with high expectations after reading lots of good reviews and after trying many of their famous items i can say that its a decent mughlai restaurant, nothing special or extraordinary, there are many mughlai joints in kolkata which serve better food than this one at kiddirpore..though its popular among locals but not worth going there from different part of the city to try their mughlai items.. Dariyabadi biriyani is good but too heavy on stomach, very rich, not for health conscious people, they don't serve naan or kulcha, only bread item available is laccha paratha which is very oily and made of dalda, fish tikka was bad, they dont use vetki, very low quality, bad smelling fish is being used for making fish tikka, chicken hariyali tikka which is supposed to be the most succulent of the kababs was very very disappointing, its not green,its almost black and no aroma or taste of coriander or mint in it, chicken peshawari kababs are small chicken legs ,white in colour like reshmi kabab & tastes like reshmi also, only gravy item we tried was mutton masala, gravy was too oily and tasteless and little sweet. it has two sections-one non ac which is like a big canteen where mainly local people eat rolls, biriyani and drink tea, another ac section where the ambiance is very  ordinary also, though its a very old restaurant and not a fine dining also still one expects some kind of good atmosphere to eat..price is cheap so if you are in the fancy market area with friends then you can visit there & eat mughlai food at cheap price but not worth going there with family in some special occasions..

##

2013-06-11 13:17:34
DrSaikat Chowdhury
904015
5.0
Ustad Ali Akbar Khan, the great Bengali " Musician of Musicians ", in an interview, once told that "Good music is like good food, it touches the hearts all over the world ".... So is the food from India Restaurant, it touches the heart. Like Pandit Nikhil Banerjee's sitar recital, it spellbounds the customers' heart throughout it course from the plate to the oesophagus. Being a doctor, I always have the opportunity to attend conferences followed by lunch/dinner in almost all the Calcutta restaurants and hotels, including all the five stars several times. In my honest opinion, this medium sized restaurant at Kidderpore offers the most delicious food of them all . Sounds overrated ? Not at all. I have come to this conclusion after 7 years of research with all the restaurants in Calcutta. Though they make wonderful Chinese preparation, I am talking about their north Indian dishes, especially the kebabs and the plain mutton biryani with a piece from the vertebral column (back). 

How to compare ? Have Mutton Biryani or Tandoori Chicken at lunch from 'India' and have the same at dinner from the place you want to compare with, you will feel the difference immediately. But if you give a 7 days gap between the two you may not make out the difference. Two kebabs, namely 'Peshawari chicken' and 'Afghani chicken' are simply heavenly. But when you take a kebab, make sure to have it between 2 pm and ask them to "make it soft". The softening of the kebab is a specialised job and depends on the man behind the Tandoor. Not everyone have the ability to "make it soft". Besides the outstanding quality, what overwhelms me, along with the people of Kidderpore-Ekbalpore, is the quantity and the price. 

No restaurant, in Calcutta, offers such a good quality food, in such a good quantity and in such a standard price( till the date of this review). If somebody finds a better place, please let me know. However, the quality of cooking may not be outstanding everyday as it depends upon several factors, and during Durga Puja and Eid, the quality falls a bit. Highly recommended for taking away a parcel and enjoy the food at office/home. If you have the taste buds of Nawab Wajid Ali Shah, the inventor of "Kalkatta Biryani" and the pioneer of biryanis and kebabs in Bengal, surely you will fall in ¬†love with the Chef.

2012-12-22 08:47:58
Samit Roychoudhury
349869
3.5
Visited on 21.12.12.
Had heard a lot about this eatery, and my first visit was worth the wait.
Had a Mutton Kachhi Biryani, which was rather good. Tasty, succulent and mildly sweet with cashew and raisin. Found it quite rich. The mutton piece was so tender and well cooked. The quantity was almost too much. The potato as usual not up to the mark (as is in most places). The egg could have been dispensed with too.
Unfortunately they had run out of Thumsup, so had to do with a Pepsi.
Ended meal with a reasonably well made gajar-ka-halwa.
While there, a waiter served tandoori chicken at another table, and the smell that wafted in made me want to try it out right then!
